## `docker-compose.yml`

المرجع يقترح فصل app عن qdrant وpostgres وredis في الإنتاج أو شبه الإنتاج، وهذا هو أقرب bootstrap عملي لهذه الفكرة.[^45_1]

```yaml
version: "3.8"

services:
  app:
    build: .
    container_name: islamic-rag-app
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    volumes:
      - ./:/app
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=sqlite:///./data/books.db
      - QDRANT_URL=http://qdrant:6333
    depends_on:
      - qdrant

  qdrant:
    image: qdrant/qdrant:latest
    container_name: islamic-rag-qdrant
    ports:
      - "6333:6333"
    volumes:
      - qdrant_data:/qdrant/storage

  redis:
    image: redis:alpine
    container_name: islamic-rag-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"

volumes:
  qdrant_data:
```


## `Dockerfile`

```dockerfile
FROM python:3.10-slim

WORKDIR /app

RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git curl && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

COPY requirements.txt .
RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt

COPY . .

RUN mkdir -p /app/data/vectorstore /app/data/metadata

EXPOSE 8000

CMD ["uvicorn", "app.main:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "8000"]
```


## `tests/test_api.py`

المرجع يتكلم بوضوح عن test coverage لأساسيات الـ API والـ RAG pipeline، وأول خطوة هنا هي التأكد أن health والmetadata endpoints وqa endpoint لا تنهار.[^45_1]

```python
from fastapi.testclient import TestClient
from app.main import app

client = TestClient(app)

def test_root():
    response = client.get("/")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    body = response.json()
    assert body["status"] == "ok"

def test_health():
    response = client.get("/health")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert response.json()["status"] == "healthy"

def test_categories_endpoint():
    response = client.get("/categories")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert isinstance(response.json(), list)

def test_books_search_endpoint():
    response = client.get("/books/search")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert isinstance(response.json(), list)

def test_authors_search_endpoint():
    response = client.get("/authors/search")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    assert isinstance(response.json(), list)

def test_qa_ask_endpoint():
    payload = {"query": "ما حكم الزكاة؟"}
    response = client.post("/qa/ask", json=payload)
    assert response.status_code == 200
    body = response.json()
    assert "answer" in body
    assert "intent" in body
    assert "citations" in body
```


## `tests/test_router.py`

بما أن المعمارية كلها تبدأ من routing، فهذا الاختبار من أهم الاختبارات المبكرة، خصوصًا للـ GUID والـ short ID وzakat routing.[^45_1]

```python
from app.agents.router import RouterAgent

def test_guid_detection():
    router = RouterAgent()
    result = router.classify("ابحث عن الكتاب ace0dc28-7030-5890-8962-fdaf7a448647")
    assert result.requires_retrieval is False
    assert result.entities["guid"] == "ace0dc28-7030-5890-8962-fdaf7a448647"

def test_shortid_detection():
    router = RouterAgent()
    result = router.classify("هات الكتاب 6B86B2")
    assert result.requires_retrieval is False
    assert result.entities["shortid"].upper() == "6B86B2"

def test_zakat_intent():
    router = RouterAgent()
    result = router.classify("كم زكاة 100000 جنيه")
    assert result.intent == "ZAKAT"
    assert result.next_action == "calculator"
```


## `tests/test_retrieval.py`

```python
from app.services.planner import RetrievalPlanner
from app.models.schemas import UserIntent

def test_retrieval_plan_default():
    planner = RetrievalPlanner()
    intent = UserIntent(
        intent="FIQH",
        confidence=0.8,
        requires_retrieval=True,
        reasoning="test",
        next_action="retrieval",
    )
    plan = planner.create_plan(intent)
    assert plan.mode == "rag"
    assert plan.extractedonly is True
```


## أوامر التشغيل

أبسط path للتشغيل الآن:

```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
cp .env.example .env
python -m app.ingestion.loadsqlite
uvicorn app.main:app --reload
```

وبعدها تفتح `/docs`، وهذا هو المسار نفسه تقريبًا الذي يقترحه المرجع لبدء التشغيل المحلي بعد التحضير والتحميل.[^45_1]

## ما الذي أصبح جاهزًا الآن

بهذه الملفات صار عندك:

- metadata DB bootstrap من ملفاتك الحالية.[^45_2][^45_1]
- FastAPI app قابلة للإقلاع.[^45_1]
- Router أولي + graph state + tests أولية.[^45_1]
- docker وenv وrequirements كبداية تشغيل محترمة.[^45_1]

الشيء التالي المنطقي الآن هو أن أكتب لك **المرحلة التالية كاملة بالكود**:

- `services/vectorstore.py`
- `agents/answeragent.py`
- `api/qa.py` نسخة أذكى فيها `/plan` و`/retrieve`
- `repositories/guidindex.py`
- `api/auth.py` و`core/security.py`

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^45_1]: chat-Islamic-RAG-Construction-1.txt

[^45_2]: README.md


---

# كمل

تمام، نكمل بالمرحلة التي تجعل المشروع **يشتغل فعليًا كـ RAG skeleton**: vector store، answer agent، GUID repository، auth/security، وQA endpoints فيها `/plan` و`/retrieve` و`/ask`. هذا متوافق مع المرجع الذي يضع vector retrieval + answer generation + citation validation + auth فوق metadata layer الحالية عندك.[^46_1][^46_2]

## `app/repositories/guidindex.py`

بما أن عندك `guidindex.json` مخصص للـ fast lookup، فمن الأفضل استخدام repository بسيط يقرأه في الذاكرة بدل تنفيذ scan على `books.json` أو الاعتماد على SQL في كل مرة، خصوصًا لمسارات GUID وshort ID.[^46_2][^46_1]

```python
import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any

class GUIDIndexRepository:
    def __init__(self, file_path: str = "data/metadata/guidindex.json"):
        self.file_path = Path(file_path)
        self.data = self._load()

    def _load(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if not self.file_path.exists():
            return {}
        with open(self.file_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            return json.load(f)

    def get_by_guid(self, guid: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        guids = self.data.get("guids", self.data)
        return guids.get(guid)

    def get_by_shortid(self, shortid: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        shortid = shortid.upper()
        guids = self.data.get("guids", self.data)
        for _, value in guids.items():
            if (value.get("short") or value.get("shortid") or "").upper() == shortid:
                return value
        return None
```


## `app/core/security.py`

المرجع يقترح JWT-based auth باستخدام `python-jose`, `passlib`, و`OAuth2PasswordBearer`، وهذا يكفي جدًا للنسخة الأولى من API.[^46_1]

```python
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Optional

from jose import JWTError, jwt
from passlib.context import CryptContext
from fastapi import Depends, HTTPException, status
from fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordBearer
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.config import settings
from app.core.db import get_db
from app.models.dbmodels import User

pwd_context = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")
oauth2_scheme = OAuth2PasswordBearer(tokenUrl="/auth/login")

def verify_password(plain_password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:
    return pwd_context.verify(plain_password, hashed_password)

def get_password_hash(password: str) -> str:
    return pwd_context.hash(password)

def create_access_token(data: dict, expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:
    to_encode = data.copy()
    expire = datetime.utcnow() + (expires_delta or timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES))
    to_encode.update({"exp": expire})
    return jwt.encode(to_encode, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)

def decode_access_token(token: str) -> Optional[dict]:
    try:
        return jwt.decode(token, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.ALGORITHM])
    except JWTError:
        return None

def get_current_user(token: str = Depends(oauth2_scheme), db: Session = Depends(get_db)) -> User:
    credentials_exception = HTTPException(
        status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
        detail="Could not validate credentials",
        headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
    )
    payload = decode_access_token(token)
    if payload is None:
        raise credentials_exception

    username = payload.get("sub")
    if not username:
        raise credentials_exception

    user = db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first()
    if user is None:
        raise credentials_exception

    return user
```


## تعديل `app/models/dbmodels.py`

حتى يعمل auth فعليًا، أضف `User` وربط `QueryLog` بالمستخدم، وهو أيضًا متوافق مع الـ schema الممتد المقترح في المرجع.[^46_1]

```python
class User(Base):
    __tablename__ = "users"

    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)
    username = Column(String(64), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    email = Column(String(128), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    hashedpassword = Column(String(256), nullable=False)
    isactive = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    issuperuser = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    createdat = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updatedat = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)

    queries = relationship("QueryLog", back_populates="user")

# داخل QueryLog
userid = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"), index=True, nullable=True)
user = relationship("User", back_populates="queries")
```


## تعديل `app/models/schemas.py`

أضف schemas الخاصة بالمستخدم وtoken لأنها جزء من API auth المقترح في المرجع.[^46_1]

```python
class UserCreate(BaseModel):
    username: str
    email: str
    password: str

class UserResponse(BaseModel):
    id: int
    username: str
    email: str
    isactive: bool

    class Config:
        from_attributes = True

class Token(BaseModel):
    access_token: str
    token_type: str
```


## `app/api/auth.py`

هذه endpoints الأساسية: register, login, me، وهي نفس الثلاثية الطبيعية في هذا النوع من المشاريع.[^46_1]

```python
from datetime import timedelta
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status
from fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordRequestForm
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import get_db
from app.core.config import settings
from app.core.security import verify_password, get_password_hash, create_access_token, get_current_user
from app.models.dbmodels import User
from app.models.schemas import UserCreate, UserResponse, Token

router = APIRouter(prefix="/auth", tags=["auth"])

@router.post("/register", response_model=UserResponse)
def register(userdata: UserCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    existing = db.query(User).filter(
        (User.username == userdata.username) | (User.email == userdata.email)
    ).first()

    if existing:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Username or email already registered")

    user = User(
        username=userdata.username,
        email=userdata.email,
        hashedpassword=get_password_hash(userdata.password),
    )
    db.add(user)
    db.commit()
    db.refresh(user)
    return user

@router.post("/login", response_model=Token)
def login(form_data: OAuth2PasswordRequestForm = Depends(), db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    user = db.query(User).filter(User.username == form_data.username).first()
    if not user or not verify_password(form_data.password, user.hashedpassword):
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
            detail="Incorrect username or password",
            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
        )

    access_token = create_access_token(
        data={"sub": user.username},
        expires_delta=timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES),
    )
    return {"access_token": access_token, "token_type": "bearer"}

@router.get("/me", response_model=UserResponse)
def me(current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)):
    return current_user
```


## `app/services/vectorstore.py`

المرجع يقترح Qdrant + SentenceTransformers + payload filtering بالـ book/category/author/extracted، وهذا بالضبط ما تحتاجه حتى يظل retrieval metadata-aware بدل semantic search أعمى.[^46_1]

```python
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional

from qdrant_client import QdrantClient
from qdrant_client.http.models import (
    Distance,
    VectorParams,
    PointStruct,
    Filter,
    FieldCondition,
    MatchValue,
    MatchAny,
)
from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer

from app.core.config import settings

class VectorStoreService:
    def __init__(self):
        self.client = QdrantClient(url=settings.QDRANT_URL, api_key=settings.QDRANT_API_KEY)
        self.embedding_model = SentenceTransformer(settings.EMBEDDING_MODEL)
        self.collection_name = "islamic_books"
        self.vector_size = len(self.embedding_model.encode("test"))
        self._create_collection_if_not_exists()

    def _create_collection_if_not_exists(self):
        collections = self.client.get_collections().collections
        names = [c.name for c in collections]
        if self.collection_name not in names:
            self.client.create_collection(
                collection_name=self.collection_name,
                vectors_config=VectorParams(size=self.vector_size, distance=Distance.COSINE),
            )
            self.client.create_payload_index(self.collection_name, "bookid", "integer")
            self.client.create_payload_index(self.collection_name, "categoryid", "integer")
            self.client.create_payload_index(self.collection_name, "authorids", "integer")
            self.client.create_payload_index(self.collection_name, "extracted", "bool")

    def add_chunks(self, chunks: List[Dict[str, Any]], batch_size: int = 100):
        points = []
        for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
            vector = self.embedding_model.encode(chunk["text"]).tolist()
            points.append(
                PointStruct(
                    id=i,
                    vector=vector,
                    payload=chunk,
                )
            )
            if len(points) >= batch_size:
                self.client.upsert(collection_name=self.collection_name, points=points)
                points = []

        if points:
            self.client.upsert(collection_name=self.collection_name, points=points)

    def _build_filter(self, filter_dict: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Optional[Filter]:
        if not filter_dict:
            return None

        conditions = []

        if filter_dict.get("bookids"):
            conditions.append(FieldCondition(key="bookid", match=MatchAny(any=filter_dict["bookids"])))
        if filter_dict.get("authorids"):
            conditions.append(FieldCondition(key="authorids", match=MatchAny(any=filter_dict["authorids"])))
        if filter_dict.get("categoryids"):
            conditions.append(FieldCondition(key="categoryid", match=MatchAny(any=filter_dict["categoryids"])))
        if filter_dict.get("extractedonly"):
            conditions.append(FieldCondition(key="extracted", match=MatchValue(value=True)))

        if not conditions:
            return None

        return Filter(must=conditions)

    def search(self, query: str, k: int = None, filter_dict: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        k = k or settings.TOP_K
        query_vector = self.embedding_model.encode(query).tolist()
        qdrant_filter = self._build_filter(filter_dict)

        results = self.client.search(
            collection_name=self.collection_name,
            query_vector=query_vector,
            query_filter=qdrant_filter,
            limit=k,
            with_payload=True,
            with_vectors=False,
        )

        formatted = []
        for result in results:
            payload = result.payload
            formatted.append({
                "chunkid": payload.get("chunkid"),
                "bookid": payload.get("bookid"),
                "bookguid": payload.get("bookguid"),
                "booktitle": payload.get("booktitle"),
                "categoryid": payload.get("categoryid"),
                "categoryname": payload.get("categoryname"),
                "chunkindex": payload.get("chunkindex"),
                "text": payload.get("text"),
                "score": result.score,
            })
        return formatted
```


## `app/services/citationvalidator.py`

المرجع يوصي صراحة بمرحلة citation validation حتى لا تعرض citations لا علاقة لها بالإجابة أو بالسياق.[^46_1]

```python
from typing import List, Dict, Any

class CitationValidator:
    def validate(self, answer: str, chunks: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        valid = []
        for chunk in chunks:
            if chunk.get("text") and len(chunk["text"]) > 20:
                valid.append({
                    "bookid": chunk.get("bookid"),
                    "booktitle": chunk.get("booktitle", ""),
                    "bookguid": chunk.get("bookguid", ""),
                    "chunkid": chunk.get("chunkid", ""),
                    "chunkindex": chunk.get("chunkindex", 0),
                    "text": chunk.get("text", "")[:280],
                    "relevancescore": chunk.get("score", 0.0),
                })
        return valid
```


## `app/agents/answeragent.py`

في أول نسخة لا تجعل الـ answer agent معقدًا جدًا؛ يكفي أن يبني prompt من أفضل chunks ويُرجع answer + citations. هذا متسق مع الهيكل المرجعي الذي يفصل `build_context -> create_prompt -> extract_citations`.[^46_1]

```python
from typing import List, Dict, Any
from pydantic import BaseModel

from app.services.citationvalidator import CitationValidator

class AnswerResult(BaseModel):
    answer: str
    citations: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    confidence: float

class AnswerAgent:
    def __init__(self, llm=None):
        self.llm = llm
        self.validator = CitationValidator()

    def build_context(self, chunks: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
        parts = []
        for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks[:5], start=1):
            parts.append(f"[C{i}] {chunk.get('booktitle', 'Unknown')}\n{chunk.get('text', '')}")
        return "\n\n".join(parts)

    def generate(self, query: str, chunks: List[Dict[str, Any]], intent: Dict[str, Any] | None = None) -> AnswerResult:
        if not chunks:
            return AnswerResult(
                answer="لم يتم العثور على سياق كافٍ للإجابة بشكل موثوق.",
                citations=[],
                confidence=0.2,
            )

        context = self.build_context(chunks)

        if self.llm is None:
            answer = f"إجابة أولية مبنية على {len(chunks)} مقاطع مسترجعة. يلزم توصيل LLM لاحقًا لإنتاج جواب نهائي.\n\n{context[:1200]}"
        else:
            prompt = f"""
أنت مساعد بحث إسلامي عربي.
أجب اعتمادًا فقط على السياق التالي، واذكر عند عدم كفاية المعلومات.

السؤال:
{query}

السياق:
{context}

أجب بالعربية الفصحى باختصار ووضوح.
"""
            answer = self.llm.invoke(prompt)

        citations = self.validator.validate(answer, chunks[:5])
        confidence = min(0.95, 0.5 + (0.08 * len(citations)))
        return AnswerResult(answer=answer, citations=citations, confidence=confidence)
```


## `app/api/qa.py`

هذا الملف يجب أن يعرض ثلاث طبقات:

- `/plan` لعرض قرار النظام قبل retrieval
- `/retrieve` لعرض chunks والخطة
- `/ask` لعرض answer النهائي مع logging
وهذا يتماشى مباشرة مع المرجع.[^46_1]

```python
import json
import time
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, BackgroundTasks
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import get_db
from app.core.security import get_current_user
from app.models.dbmodels import QueryLog, User
from app.models.schemas import QueryRequest, QueryResponse, UserIntent
from app.agents.router import RouterAgent
from app.services.planner import RetrievalPlanner
from app.services.vectorstore import VectorStoreService
from app.agents.answeragent import AnswerAgent

router = APIRouter(prefix="/qa", tags=["qa"])

router_agent = RouterAgent()
planner = RetrievalPlanner()
vectorstore = VectorStoreService()
answer_agent = AnswerAgent()

def log_query(db: Session, userid: int | None, query: str, result: dict, latencyms: float):
    row = QueryLog(
        userid=userid,
        query=query,
        intent=result.get("intent", {}).get("intent"),
        confidence=result.get("confidence"),
        response=result.get("answer"),
        latencyms=latencyms,
        citations=json.dumps(result.get("citations", []), ensure_ascii=False),
    )
    db.add(row)
    db.commit()

@router.post("/plan")
def create_plan(request: QueryRequest):
    intent = router_agent.classify(request.query)
    plan = planner.create_plan(intent)

    if request.bookids:
        plan.bookids = request.bookids
    if request.authorids:
        plan.authorids = request.authorids
    if request.categoryids:
        plan.categoryids = request.categoryids

    return {
        "intent": intent.model_dump(),
        "plan": plan.model_dump(),
    }

@router.post("/retrieve")
def retrieve_docs(request: QueryRequest):
    intent = router_agent.classify(request.query)
    plan = planner.create_plan(intent)

    if request.bookids:
        plan.bookids = request.bookids
    if request.authorids:
        plan.authorids = request.authorids
    if request.categoryids:
        plan.categoryids = request.categoryids

    chunks = vectorstore.search(
        query=request.query,
        k=10,
        filter_dict=plan.model_dump(),
    )

    return {
        "query": request.query,
        "intent": intent.model_dump(),
        "plan": plan.model_dump(),
        "chunks": chunks,
    }

@router.post("/ask", response_model=QueryResponse)
def ask_question(
    request: QueryRequest,
    background_tasks: BackgroundTasks,
    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
    current_user: User | None = Depends(get_current_user),
):
    start = time.time()

    intent = router_agent.classify(request.query)
    plan = planner.create_plan(intent)

    if request.bookids:
        plan.bookids = request.bookids
    if request.authorids:
        plan.authorids = request.authorids
    if request.categoryids:
        plan.categoryids = request.categoryids

    chunks = []
    if intent.requires_retrieval:
        chunks = vectorstore.search(
            query=request.query,
            k=10,
            filter_dict=plan.model_dump(),
        )

    result = answer_agent.generate(
        query=request.query,
        chunks=chunks,
        intent=intent.model_dump(),
    )

    latencyms = (time.time() - start) * 1000

    payload = {
        "answer": result.answer,
        "intent": intent.model_dump(),
        "citations": result.citations,
        "confidence": result.confidence,
    }

    background_tasks.add_task(
        log_query,
        db,
        current_user.id if current_user else None,
        request.query,
        payload,
        latencyms,
    )

    return QueryResponse(
        answer=result.answer,
        intent=UserIntent(**intent.model_dump()),
        citations=result.citations,
        confidence=result.confidence,
        latencyms=latencyms,
    )
```


## تعديل صغير مهم على `/ask`

لو أردت أن يكون auth **اختياريًا** في `/ask` بدل إجباري، فافصل dependency الحالية لأن `OAuth2PasswordBearer` يرفع 401 تلقائيًا. في النسخة الحالية endpoint يعتبر محميًا، وهذا مناسب لو API داخلية.[^46_1]

## تعديل `app/main.py`

أدخل auth router بالإضافة إلى routers السابقة.[^46_1]

```python
from fastapi import FastAPI
from app.core.db import Base, engine
from app.api import books, authors, categories, qa, auth

Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)

app = FastAPI(title="Islamic RAG System", version="1.0.0")

app.include_router(auth.router)
app.include_router(books.router)
app.include_router(authors.router)
app.include_router(categories.router)
app.include_router(qa.router)

@app.get("/")
def root():
    return {"name": "Islamic RAG System", "status": "ok"}

@app.get("/health")
def health():
    return {"status": "healthy"}
```


## كيف تستخدمه الآن

الـ flow أصبح كالتالي:

1. `POST /auth/register`
2. `POST /auth/login`
3. انسخ `access_token`
4. جرّب `POST /qa/plan`
5. ثم `POST /qa/retrieve`
6. ثم `POST /qa/ask`
وهذا يطابق تقريبًا تدفق “classify -> plan -> retrieve -> answer -> log” الموصى به في المرجع.[^46_1]

## أهم ملاحظة مع بياناتك

لأن عندك `8,425` كتابًا تقريبًا، و`8,423` منها مستخرجة نصيًا، و`3,146` مؤلفًا، و`41` تصنيفًا، فأفضل خطوة بعد هذا bootstrap هي **ingest chunks مع payload metadata كاملة**: `bookid`, `bookguid`, `booktitle`, `authorids`, `categoryid`, `extracted`, `sourcefile`، لأن هذه هي المفاتيح التي تجعل التصفية قبل retrieval فعالة فعلًا على corpus الحقيقي.[^46_2][^46_1]

## المرحلة التالية

الشيء التالي المناسب الآن هو أن أكمل لك **طبقة ingestion إلى Qdrant بالكامل**:

- script لقراءة `extractedbooks/*.txt`
- ربط كل ملف بصف الكتاب من `books.db`
- chunking + payload enrichment
- upsert إلى Qdrant
- endpoint أو command لإعادة index كتاب واحد أو مجموعة كتب فقط

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^46_1]: chat-Islamic-RAG-Construction-1.txt

[^46_2]: README.md


---

# كمل

ممتاز، نكمل الآن بطبقة **ingestion إلى Qdrant** لأنها الجزء الذي يحول الـ architecture من spec إلى نظام قابل للتشغيل على corpus الحقيقي عندك. هذا مناسب جدًا لبياناتك لأن عندك `books.db` للعلاقات والاستعلام، و`extractedbooks/*.txt` للنصوص، وقرابة `8,423` كتابًا مستخرجًا من أصل `8,425`، وبالتالي أفضل خط ingest هو: `SQLite metadata -> text file -> chunking -> payload enrichment -> Qdrant upsert`.[^47_1][^47_2]

## المسار المقترح

اجعل ingestion منفصلًا عن الـ API runtime، بحيث تكون عندك scripts أو services لـ:

- تحميل metadata من `books.db`.
- قراءة النص من `extractedbooks/{file}` أو `{bookid}.txt`.
- chunking مع overlap.
- تجهيز payload غني فيه `bookid`, `bookguid`, `booktitle`, `authorids`, `categoryid`, `extracted`, `sourcefile`.
- حذف vectors القديمة للكتاب عند reindex.
- upsert إلى Qdrant batches.
هذا يتوافق مع المرجع الذي يفصل `ingestion/`, `chunkprocessor.py`, و`IngestionPipeline` عن طبقة الـ API والـ agents.[^47_1]


## `app/ingestion/chunker.py`

ابدأ بـ chunker بسيط وعملي. المرجع يقترح chunk size حوالي 512 وoverlap 50، وهذا مناسب كبداية لكتب عربية طويلة قبل أي tuning لاحق.[^47_1]

```python
import re
from typing import List, Dict, Any

class ArabicChunker:
    def __init__(self, chunk_size: int = 1200, overlap: int = 150, min_chunk_len: int = 80):
        self.chunk_size = chunk_size
        self.overlap = overlap
        self.min_chunk_len = min_chunk_len
        self.separators = ["\n\n", "\n", "۔", ".", "؟", "!", "؛"]

    def normalize_text(self, text: str) -> str:
        text = text.replace("\ufeff", " ")
        text = re.sub(r"\r\n?", "\n", text)
        text = re.sub(r"[ \t]+", " ", text)
        text = re.sub(r"\n{3,}", "\n\n", text)
        return text.strip()

    def split_text(self, text: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        text = self.normalize_text(text)
        chunks = []

        start = 0
        while start < len(text):
            end = min(start + self.chunk_size, len(text))

            if end < len(text):
                best_end = end
                for sep in self.separators:
                    pos = text.rfind(sep, start, end)
                    if pos > start + (self.chunk_size // 2):
                        best_end = pos + len(sep)
                        break
                end = best_end

            chunk_text = text[start:end].strip()
            if len(chunk_text) >= self.min_chunk_len:
                chunks.append({
                    "text": chunk_text,
                    "startoffset": start,
                    "endoffset": end,
                    "textlen": len(chunk_text),
                })

            if end >= len(text):
                break

            start = max(end - self.overlap, 0)

        return chunks
```


## `app/ingestion/metadata_loader.py`

استخدم `books.db` كمصدر الحقيقة الأساسي، لأن README يوضح أن هذا الملف يحتوي `books`, `authors`, و`bookauthors` بشكل queryable، وهو الأفضل من تحميل JSON كامل في ingestion loop.[^47_2]

```python
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from sqlalchemy import text

class MetadataLoader:
    def __init__(self, db: Session):
        self.db = db

    def get_book_metadata(self, bookid: int) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        row = self.db.execute(text("""
            SELECT 
                b.bookid,
                b.guid,
                b.shortid,
                b.title,
                b.catid,
                b.catname,
                b.date,
                b.authorstr,
                b.extracted,
                b.file,
                b.sizemb
            FROM books b
            WHERE b.bookid = :bookid
        """), {"bookid": bookid}).mappings().first()

        if not row:
            return None

        authors = self.db.execute(text("""
            SELECT a.authorid, a.guid, a.shortid, a.name, a.death, ba.role
            FROM bookauthors ba
            JOIN authors a ON a.authorid = ba.authorid
            WHERE ba.bookid = :bookid
            ORDER BY a.authorid
        """), {"bookid": bookid}).mappings().all()

        return {
            "bookid": row["bookid"],
            "guid": row["guid"],
            "shortid": row["shortid"],
            "title": row["title"],
            "categoryid": row["catid"],
            "categoryname": row["catname"],
            "datehijri": row["date"],
            "authorstr": row["authorstr"],
            "extracted": bool(row["extracted"]),
            "file": row["file"],
            "sizemb": row["sizemb"],
            "authors": [dict(a) for a in authors],
            "authorids": [a["authorid"] for a in authors],
            "authorguids": [a["guid"] for a in authors if a["guid"]],
            "authornames": [a["name"] for a in authors if a["name"]],
        }

    def list_extracted_books(self, start_id: int = 1, end_id: Optional[int] = None) -> List[int]:
        sql = """
            SELECT bookid
            FROM books
            WHERE extracted = 1
        """
        params = {}

        if end_id is not None:
            sql += " AND bookid BETWEEN :start_id AND :end_id"
            params = {"start_id": start_id, "end_id": end_id}
        else:
            sql += " AND bookid >= :start_id"
            params = {"start_id": start_id}

        sql += " ORDER BY bookid"
        rows = self.db.execute(text(sql), params).fetchall()
        return [r[^47_0] for r in rows]
```


## `app/ingestion/text_loader.py`

بما أن README يذكر أن لكل كتاب ملف نصي مستخرج مثل `1.txt`, `2.txt`… فمن الأفضل أن تقرأ الملف من الحقل `file` إن وجد، وتستخدم fallback إلى `{bookid}.txt` عند الحاجة.[^47_2]

```python
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional

class ExtractedTextLoader:
    def __init__(self, extracted_dir: str = "data/extractedbooks"):
        self.extracted_dir = Path(extracted_dir)

    def resolve_file_path(self, book_meta: dict) -> Optional[Path]:
        candidates = []

        if book_meta.get("file"):
            candidates.append(self.extracted_dir / str(book_meta["file"]))

        if book_meta.get("bookid"):
            candidates.append(self.extracted_dir / f"{book_meta['bookid']}.txt")

        for path in candidates:
            if path.exists():
                return path

        return None

    def load_text(self, book_meta: dict) -> Optional[str]:
        path = self.resolve_file_path(book_meta)
        if not path:
            return None

        with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f:
            return f.read()
```


## تحسين `VectorStoreService`

أضف 3 وظائف مهمة:

- توليد point IDs ثابتة بدل `enumerate`.
- حذف vectors الخاصة بكتاب قبل reindex.
- stats بسيطة.
المرجع يذكر `delete_by_bookid()` و`get_stats()` ضمن vector store layer.[^47_1]

```python
import hashlib
from qdrant_client.http.models import FilterSelector

class VectorStoreService:
    # ... نفس الكود السابق ...

    def _stable_point_id(self, chunkid: str) -> int:
        digest = hashlib.sha256(chunkid.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()[:16]
        return int(digest, 16)

    def add_chunks(self, chunks: list[dict], batch_size: int = 100):
        points = []
        for chunk in chunks:
            vector = self.embedding_model.encode(chunk["text"]).tolist()
            points.append(
                PointStruct(
                    id=self._stable_point_id(chunk["chunkid"]),
                    vector=vector,
                    payload=chunk,
                )
            )
            if len(points) >= batch_size:
                self.client.upsert(collection_name=self.collection_name, points=points)
                points = []

        if points:
            self.client.upsert(collection_name=self.collection_name, points=points)

    def delete_by_bookid(self, bookid: int):
        self.client.delete(
            collection_name=self.collection_name,
            points_selector=FilterSelector(
                filter=Filter(
                    must=[FieldCondition(key="bookid", match=MatchValue(value=bookid))]
                )
            ),
        )

    def get_stats(self) -> dict:
        info = self.client.get_collection(self.collection_name)
        return {
            "collection_name": self.collection_name,
            "points_count": info.points_count,
            "vectors_count": info.vectors_count,
            "indexed_vectors_count": info.indexed_vectors_count,
        }
```


## `app/ingestion/pipeline.py`

هذه هي الطبقة الأهم: تجمع metadata + text + chunking + payload + upsert. المرجع يشير لنفس فكرة `IngestionPipeline` مع batch embedding و`ingest_all_extracted()`.[^47_1]

```python
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.ingestion.chunker import ArabicChunker
from app.ingestion.metadata_loader import MetadataLoader
from app.ingestion.text_loader import ExtractedTextLoader
from app.services.vectorstore import VectorStoreService

class IngestionPipeline:
    def __init__(
        self,
        db: Session,
        vectorstore: VectorStoreService,
        extracted_dir: str = "data/extractedbooks",
        chunk_size: int = 1200,
        overlap: int = 150,
    ):
        self.db = db
        self.vectorstore = vectorstore
        self.metadata_loader = MetadataLoader(db)
        self.text_loader = ExtractedTextLoader(extracted_dir)
        self.chunker = ArabicChunker(chunk_size=chunk_size, overlap=overlap)

    def _build_payloads(self, book_meta: dict, chunks: list[dict], source_file: str) -> list[dict]:
        payloads = []
        for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
            chunkid = f"{book_meta['guid']}:chunk:{i}"
            payloads.append({
                "chunkid": chunkid,
                "bookid": book_meta["bookid"],
                "bookguid": book_meta["guid"],
                "bookshortid": book_meta["shortid"],
                "booktitle": book_meta["title"],
                "categoryid": book_meta["categoryid"],
                "categoryname": book_meta["categoryname"],
                "authorids": book_meta["authorids"],
                "authorguids": book_meta["authorguids"],
                "authornames": book_meta["authornames"],
                "datehijri": book_meta["datehijri"],
                "chunkindex": i,
                "text": chunk["text"],
                "textlen": chunk["textlen"],
                "startoffset": chunk["startoffset"],
                "endoffset": chunk["endoffset"],
                "sourcefile": source_file,
                "extracted": book_meta["extracted"],
                "sourcetype": "book",
                "language": "ar",
            })
        return payloads

    def ingest_book(self, bookid: int, reindex: bool = True, batch_size: int = 100) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        book_meta = self.metadata_loader.get_book_metadata(bookid)
        if not book_meta:
            return {"ok": False, "bookid": bookid, "error": "Book metadata not found"}

        if not book_meta["extracted"]:
            return {"ok": False, "bookid": bookid, "error": "Book is not extracted"}

        text = self.text_loader.load_text(book_meta)
        if not text:
            return {"ok": False, "bookid": bookid, "error": "Extracted text file not found"}

        chunks = self.chunker.split_text(text)
        if not chunks:
            return {"ok": False, "bookid": bookid, "error": "No valid chunks produced"}

        payloads = self._build_payloads(
            book_meta=book_meta,
            chunks=chunks,
            source_file=book_meta.get("file") or f"{bookid}.txt",
        )

        if reindex:
            self.vectorstore.delete_by_bookid(bookid)

        self.vectorstore.add_chunks(payloads, batch_size=batch_size)

        return {
            "ok": True,
            "bookid": bookid,
            "guid": book_meta["guid"],
            "title": book_meta["title"],
            "chunks_created": len(payloads),
            "source_file": book_meta.get("file") or f"{bookid}.txt",
        }

    def ingest_range(self, start_id: int = 1, end_id: Optional[int] = None, limit: Optional[int] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        bookids = self.metadata_loader.list_extracted_books(start_id=start_id, end_id=end_id)
        if limit is not None:
            bookids = bookids[:limit]

        stats = {
            "processed": 0,
            "failed": 0,
            "total_chunks": 0,
            "errors": [],
        }

        for idx, bookid in enumerate(bookids, start=1):
            result = self.ingest_book(bookid)
            if result["ok"]:
                stats["processed"] += 1
                stats["total_chunks"] += result["chunks_created"]
            else:
                stats["failed"] += 1
                stats["errors"].append({"bookid": bookid, "error": result["error"]})

            if idx % 20 == 0:
                print(f"[INGEST] processed={idx} ok={stats['processed']} failed={stats['failed']} chunks={stats['total_chunks']}")

        return stats
```


## `app/ingestion/cli.py`

اعمل CLI صغير حتى تقدر:

- تعمل index لكتاب واحد.
- تعمل range.
- تعيد index.
هذا أفضل من ربط ingestion بـ endpoint منذ البداية، خصوصًا إذا corpus كبير.[^47_1]

```python
import argparse

from app.core.db import SessionLocal
from app.services.vectorstore import VectorStoreService
from app.ingestion.pipeline import IngestionPipeline

def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Islamic RAG ingestion CLI")
    parser.add_argument("--bookid", type=int, help="Index a single book by ID")
    parser.add_argument("--start-id", type=int, default=1)
    parser.add_argument("--end-id", type=int)
    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int)
    parser.add_argument("--no-reindex", action="store_true")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    db = SessionLocal()
    try:
        vectorstore = VectorStoreService()
        pipeline = IngestionPipeline(db=db, vectorstore=vectorstore)

        if args.bookid:
            result = pipeline.ingest_book(args.bookid, reindex=not args.no_reindex)
            print(result)
        else:
            stats = pipeline.ingest_range(
                start_id=args.start_id,
                end_id=args.end_id,
                limit=args.limit,
            )
            print(stats)
            print(vectorstore.get_stats())
    finally:
        db.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```


## أمر التشغيل

بعد تشغيل Qdrant وتهيئة البيئة، تقدر تبدأ كالتالي:[^47_1]

- فهرسة كتاب واحد:

```bash
python -m app.ingestion.cli --bookid 1
```

- فهرسة أول 100 كتاب:

```bash
python -m app.ingestion.cli --start-id 1 --limit 100
```

- فهرسة نطاق:

```bash
python -m app.ingestion.cli --start-id 1 --end-id 1000
```

المرجع أيضًا يوصي بتشغيل Qdrant على `localhost:6333`، واستخدام `bge-m3` أو embedding model مشابه، وهذا مناسب كإعداد أولي.[^47_1]

## API اختياري للإدارة

لو تحب تضيف admin endpoints بدل CLI فقط، اعمل ملف `app/api/admin.py` بسيط. لكن الأفضل تخليه محميًا أو superuser-only لأن ingestion عملية ثقيلة.[^47_1]

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import get_db
from app.core.security import get_current_user
from app.models.dbmodels import User
from app.services.vectorstore import VectorStoreService
from app.ingestion.pipeline import IngestionPipeline

router = APIRouter(prefix="/admin", tags=["admin"])

def require_superuser(user: User = Depends(get_current_user)) -> User:
    if not user.issuperuser:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Admin access required")
    return user

@router.post("/reindex/book/{bookid}")
def reindex_book(bookid: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db), _: User = Depends(require_superuser)):
    pipeline = IngestionPipeline(db=db, vectorstore=VectorStoreService())
    return pipeline.ingest_book(bookid, reindex=True)

@router.get("/vector/stats")
def vector_stats(_: User = Depends(require_superuser)):
    return VectorStoreService().get_stats()
```


## payload الذي أنصح به

المرجع يشدد على metadata-rich payload، وهذا ضروري جدًا حتى تقدر تعمل retrieval ذكي لاحقًا.[^47_1]
الحد الأدنى الذي يجب حفظه في كل chunk:

- `chunkid`
- `bookid`
- `bookguid`
- `bookshortid`
- `booktitle`
- `authorids`
- `authorguids`
- `authornames`
- `categoryid`
- `categoryname`
- `datehijri`
- `chunkindex`
- `text`
- `textlen`
- `startoffset`
- `endoffset`
- `sourcefile`
- `extracted`
- `language`
- `sourcetype`


## ملاحظات مهمة قبل الفهرسة الكاملة

- لا تبدأ بـ 8,423 كتابًا دفعة واحدة؛ ابدأ بـ 20–100 كتاب للتأكد أن chunk size والـ retrieval quality مناسبين.[^47_2][^47_1]
- لو لاحظت أن الاسترجاع واسع جدًا، قلل `chunk_size` أو أضف reranker قبل answer stage، والمرجع أصلًا يقترح طبقة reranking بعد vector search.[^47_1]
- احرص أن `authorids` و`categoryid` موجودان في payload لأن planner سيعتمد عليهما في filters لاحقًا داخل Qdrant.[^47_1]
- استخدم `books.db` في metadata resolution بدل الاعتماد الكامل على `books.json` أثناء runtime لأنه أسرع في queries التركيبية مثل author/category intersections.[^47_2]


## بعد هذه المرحلة

الآن صار عندك عمليًا:

- metadata layer
- auth
- qa endpoints
- vector store
- ingestion pipeline
والخطوة التالية الطبيعية هي **reranker + hybrid retrieval + LangGraph orchestration**، لأن المرجع يضع بعد retrieval مرحلة `rerank -> answer -> citations`، بل ويعرض graph واضح يربط router وmetadata agents وQdrant وanswer agent في pipeline واحد.[^47_1]

أكمل لك الآن بالمرحلة التالية: **RerankerService + RetrievalAgent + LangGraph graph builder**؟

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^47_1]: chat-Islamic-RAG-Construction-1.txt

[^47_2]: README.md


---

# كمل

ممتاز، نكمل الآن بالمرحلة التي تجعل الـ pipeline **agentic فعلاً**: reranker، retrieval agent، `GraphState`، nodes، و`LangGraph builder`. هذا بالضبط ما يقترحه المرجع: `route -> metadata agents -> retrieval plan -> vector search -> rerank -> answer` مع state واضح داخل LangGraph.[^48_1]

## `app/services/reranker.py`

المرجع يقترح CrossEncoder مثل `bge-reranker-v2-m3` لإعادة ترتيب النتائج بعد vector search، وهذا مهم لأن top-k من Qdrant وحده غالبًا لا يكفي في corpus عربي ضخم.[^48_1]

```python
from typing import List, Dict, Any
from sentence_transformers import CrossEncoder

from app.core.config import settings

class RerankerService:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = CrossEncoder(settings.RERANKER_MODEL)

    def rerank(self, query: str, documents: List[Dict[str, Any]], top_k: int = 5) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        if not documents:
            return []

        pairs = [(query, doc.get("text", "")) for doc in documents]
        scores = self.model.predict(pairs)

        ranked = []
        for doc, score in zip(documents, scores):
            item = dict(doc)
            item["rerankscore"] = float(score)
            ranked.append(item)

        ranked.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("rerankscore", 0.0), reverse=True)
        return ranked[:top_k]
```


## `app/agents/retrievalagent.py`

الأفضل أن تفصل planning عن retrieval نفسه. المرجع يعرض `RetrievalPlan` ثم `ChunkRetriever` أو `RetrievalAgent` يطبق الفلاتر على vector store.[^48_1]

```python
from typing import Dict, Any, List
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

from app.core.config import settings

class RetrievalPlan(BaseModel):
    mode: str = "metadataonly"
    bookids: List[int] = Field(default_factory=list)
    authorids: List[int] = Field(default_factory=list)
    categoryids: List[int] = Field(default_factory=list)
    extractedonly: bool = True
    intent: str | None = None

class RetrievalPlanner:
    def create_plan(
        self,
        intent: Dict[str, Any],
        book_candidates: List[Dict[str, Any]] | None = None,
        author_candidates: List[Dict[str, Any]] | None = None,
        category_candidates: List[Dict[str, Any]] | None = None,
        guid_candidate: Dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> RetrievalPlan:
        book_candidates = book_candidates or []
        author_candidates = author_candidates or []
        category_candidates = category_candidates or []

        bookids = [b["bookid"] for b in book_candidates if b.get("bookid")]
        authorids = [a["authorid"] for a in author_candidates if a.get("authorid")]
        categoryids = [c["catid"] for c in category_candidates if c.get("catid")]

        if guid_candidate and guid_candidate.get("bookid"):
            if guid_candidate["bookid"] not in bookids:
                bookids.append(guid_candidate["bookid"])

        mode = "rag" if intent.get("requiresretrieval") else "metadataonly"

        return RetrievalPlan(
            mode=mode,
            bookids=bookids,
            authorids=authorids,
            categoryids=categoryids,
            extractedonly=True,
            intent=intent.get("intent"),
        )

class RetrievalAgent:
    def __init__(self, vectorstore):
        self.vectorstore = vectorstore

    def search(self, query: str, plan: RetrievalPlan) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        if plan.mode == "metadataonly":
            return []

        filter_dict = {
            "bookids": plan.bookids,
            "authorids": plan.authorids,
            "categoryids": plan.categoryids,
            "extractedonly": plan.extractedonly,
        }

        return self.vectorstore.search(
            query=query,
            k=settings.TOP_K,
            filter_dict=filter_dict,
        )
```


## تعديل `app/models/schemas.py`

بما أن `RetrievalPlan` صار جزءًا أساسيًا من orchestration، ثبّته أيضًا في schemas المشتركة حتى تستخدمه في API بسهولة، والمرجع أصلًا يضع `RetrievalPlan` و`UserIntent` و`Citation` داخل طبقة schemas/state.[^48_1]

```python
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any, Literal
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

class UserIntent(BaseModel):
    intent: str
    confidence: float
    language: str
    requiresretrieval: bool
    subintent: Optional[str] = None
    entities: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    reasoning: str
    nextaction: str

class RetrievalPlanSchema(BaseModel):
    mode: Literal["metadataonly", "rag", "hybrid"] = "metadataonly"
    bookids: List[int] = Field(default_factory=list)
    authorids: List[int] = Field(default_factory=list)
    categoryids: List[int] = Field(default_factory=list)
    extractedonly: bool = True
    intent: Optional[str] = None

class Citation(BaseModel):
    bookid: int
    booktitle: str
    bookguid: str
    chunkid: str
    chunkindex: int
    text: str
    relevancescore: float

class QueryRequest(BaseModel):
    query: str
    categoryids: Optional[List[int]] = None
    authorids: Optional[List[int]] = None
    bookids: Optional[List[int]] = None

class QueryResponse(BaseModel):
    answer: str
    intent: Dict[str, Any]
    citations: List[Citation]
    confidence: float
    latencyms: float
```


## `app/models/agentstate.py`

المرجع يضع state واضح فيه intent، candidates، retrieval plan، chunks، reranked chunks، answer، citations، metadata إضافية. هذا مهم جدًا لأن LangGraph يصبح سهل التوسعة لاحقًا.[^48_1]

```python
from typing import TypedDict, List, Dict, Any, Optional

class GraphState(TypedDict, total=False):
    query: str
    userid: Optional[int]

    intent: Dict[str, Any]
    normalizedquery: str

    authorcandidates: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    categorycandidates: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    bookcandidates: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    guidcandidate: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]

    retrievalplan: Dict[str, Any]
    retrievalchunks: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    rerankedchunks: List[Dict[str, Any]]

    answer: str
    citations: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    confidence: float
    latencyms: float
    error: Optional[str]
```


## `app/graph/nodes.py`

هنا نربط الـ agents داخل nodes مستقلة. المرجع يعرض nodes لـ route, author, category, book, guid, plan, retrieve, rerank, answer.[^48_1]

```python
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.agents.router import RouterAgent
from app.agents.authoragent import AuthorAgent
from app.agents.categoryagent import CategoryAgent
from app.agents.bookagent import BookAgent
from app.agents.guidagent import GUIDAgent
from app.agents.retrievalagent import RetrievalPlanner, RetrievalAgent
from app.agents.answeragent import AnswerAgent
from app.services.reranker import RerankerService

router_agent = RouterAgent()
author_agent = AuthorAgent()
category_agent = CategoryAgent()
book_agent = BookAgent()
guid_agent = GUIDAgent()
planner = RetrievalPlanner()
reranker = RerankerService()

def route_node(state):
    query = state["query"]
    intent = router_agent.classify(query)
    return {
        "intent": intent.model_dump(),
        "normalizedquery": query.strip(),
    }

def author_node(state, db: Session):
    query = state["query"]
    intent = state.get("intent", {})
    candidates = author_agent.resolve(db, query, intent)
    return {"authorcandidates": candidates}

def category_node(state, db: Session):
    query = state["query"]
    intent = state.get("intent", {})
    candidates = category_agent.resolve(db, query, intent)
    return {"categorycandidates": candidates}

def book_node(state, db: Session):
    author_candidates = state.get("authorcandidates", [])
    category_candidates = state.get("categorycandidates", [])
    intent = state.get("intent", {})

    authorids = [a["authorid"] for a in author_candidates if a.get("authorid")]
    categoryids = [c["catid"] for c in category_candidates if c.get("catid")]

    candidates = book_agent.find_books(
        db=db,
        authorids=authorids,
        categoryids=categoryids,
        intent=intent,
    )
    return {"bookcandidates": candidates}

def guid_node(state, db: Session):
    intent = state.get("intent", {})
    entities = intent.get("entities", {})
    guid_or_shortid = entities.get("guid") or entities.get("shortid")

    if not guid_or_shortid:
        return {"guidcandidate": None}

    candidate = guid_agent.resolve(db, guid_or_shortid)
    return {"guidcandidate": candidate}

def plan_node(state):
    plan = planner.create_plan(
        intent=state.get("intent", {}),
        book_candidates=state.get("bookcandidates", []),
        author_candidates=state.get("authorcandidates", []),
        category_candidates=state.get("categorycandidates", []),
        guid_candidate=state.get("guidcandidate"),
    )
    return {"retrievalplan": plan.model_dump()}

def retrieve_node(state, vectorstore):
    query = state["query"]
    plan_dict = state.get("retrievalplan", {})
    from app.agents.retrievalagent import RetrievalPlan
    plan = RetrievalPlan(**plan_dict)

    retrieval_agent = RetrievalAgent(vectorstore=vectorstore)
    chunks = retrieval_agent.search(query, plan)
    return {"retrievalchunks": chunks}

def rerank_node(state):
    query = state["query"]
    chunks = state.get("retrievalchunks", [])
    if not chunks:
        return {"rerankedchunks": []}

    ranked = reranker.rerank(query=query, documents=chunks, top_k=5)
    return {"rerankedchunks": ranked}

def answer_node(state, llm=None):
    query = state["query"]
    intent = state.get("intent", {})
    chunks = state.get("rerankedchunks") or state.get("retrievalchunks") or []

    answer_agent = AnswerAgent(llm=llm)
    result = answer_agent.generate(query=query, chunks=chunks, intent=intent)

    return {
        "answer": result.answer,
        "citations": result.citations,
        "confidence": result.confidence,
    }
```


## `app/graph/builder.py`

المرجع يقترح `StateGraph` مع edges ثابتة وconditional routing من route إلى guid أو author chain أو مباشرة plan حسب intent/entities.[^48_1]

```python
from typing import Literal
from langgraph.graph import StateGraph, END

from app.models.agentstate import GraphState
from app.graph.nodes import (
    route_node,
    author_node,
    category_node,
    book_node,
    guid_node,
    plan_node,
    retrieve_node,
    rerank_node,
    answer_node,
)

def build_graph(db, vectorstore, llm=None):
    graph = StateGraph(GraphState)

    graph.add_node("route", route_node)
    graph.add_node("author", lambda state: author_node(state, db))
    graph.add_node("category", lambda state: category_node(state, db))
    graph.add_node("book", lambda state: book_node(state, db))
    graph.add_node("guid", lambda state: guid_node(state, db))
    graph.add_node("plan", plan_node)
    graph.add_node("retrieve", lambda state: retrieve_node(state, vectorstore))
    graph.add_node("rerank", rerank_node)
    graph.add_node("answer", lambda state: answer_node(state, llm))

    graph.set_entry_point("route")

    def route_decision(state) -> Literal["guid", "author", "plan"]:
        intent = state.get("intent", {})
        entities = intent.get("entities", {})

        if entities.get("guid") or entities.get("shortid"):
            return "guid"

        if intent.get("requiresretrieval", False):
            return "author"

        return "plan"

    graph.add_conditional_edges(
        "route",
        route_decision,
        {
            "guid": "guid",
            "author": "author",
            "plan": "plan",
        },
    )

    graph.add_edge("author", "category")
    graph.add_edge("category", "book")
    graph.add_edge("book", "plan")
    graph.add_edge("guid", "plan")
    graph.add_edge("plan", "retrieve")
    graph.add_edge("retrieve", "rerank")
    graph.add_edge("rerank", "answer")
    graph.add_edge("answer", END)

    return graph.compile()
```


## كيف يشتغل هذا فعليًا

التدفق أصبح كالتالي:[^48_1]

- **route**: يصنف السؤال ويستخرج entities مثل GUID أو short ID أو intent عام.
- **author/category/book**: يبني candidate space من metadata layer.
- **plan**: يكوّن retrieval filters مثل `bookids`, `authorids`, `categoryids`, `extractedonly=True`.
- **retrieve**: يعمل vector search داخل Qdrant مع payload filters.
- **rerank**: يعيد ترتيب أفضل المقاطع.
- **answer**: يصيغ الجواب ويخرج citations.
هذا يطابق بشكل مباشر الرسم المعماري الموجود في المرجع للـ multi-agent RAG.[^48_1]


## تعديل `app/api/qa.py` ليستخدم graph

بدل استدعاء planner وvector store يدويًا داخل كل endpoint، الأفضل الآن استخدام graph مباشرة، وهذا هو نفس التوجه الموجود في المرجع لـ `/retrieve` و`/ask`.[^48_1]

```python
import json
import time
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, BackgroundTasks
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import get_db
from app.core.security import get_current_user
from app.models.dbmodels import QueryLog, User
from app.models.schemas import QueryRequest, QueryResponse
from app.graph.builder import build_graph
from app.services.vectorstore import VectorStoreService

router = APIRouter(prefix="/qa", tags=["qa"])
vectorstore = VectorStoreService()

def log_query(db: Session, userid: int | None, query: str, result: dict, latencyms: float):
    row = QueryLog(
        userid=userid,
        query=query,
        intent=result.get("intent", {}).get("intent"),
        confidence=result.get("confidence"),
        response=result.get("answer"),
        latencyms=latencyms,
        citations=json.dumps(result.get("citations", []), ensure_ascii=False),
    )
    db.add(row)
    db.commit()

@router.post("/plan")
def create_plan(request: QueryRequest, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    graph = build_graph(db=db, vectorstore=vectorstore, llm=None)
    result = graph.invoke({"query": request.query})
    return {
        "query": request.query,
        "intent": result.get("intent", {}),
        "plan": result.get("retrievalplan", {}),
        "bookcandidates": result.get("bookcandidates", []),
        "authorcandidates": result.get("authorcandidates", []),
        "categorycandidates": result.get("categorycandidates", []),
        "guidcandidate": result.get("guidcandidate"),
    }

@router.post("/retrieve")
def retrieve_docs(request: QueryRequest, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    graph = build_graph(db=db, vectorstore=vectorstore, llm=None)
    result = graph.invoke({"query": request.query})
    return {
        "query": request.query,
        "intent": result.get("intent", {}),
        "plan": result.get("retrievalplan", {}),
        "chunks": result.get("retrievalchunks", []),
        "rerankedchunks": result.get("rerankedchunks", []),
    }

@router.post("/ask", response_model=QueryResponse)
def ask_question(
    request: QueryRequest,
    background_tasks: BackgroundTasks,
    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
    current_user: User | None = Depends(get_current_user),
):
    start = time.time()
    graph = build_graph(db=db, vectorstore=vectorstore, llm=None)
    result = graph.invoke({
        "query": request.query,
        "userid": current_user.id if current_user else None,
    })
    latencyms = (time.time() - start) * 1000

    background_tasks.add_task(
        log_query,
        db,
        current_user.id if current_user else None,
        request.query,
        result,
        latencyms,
    )

    return QueryResponse(
        answer=result.get("answer", ""),
        intent=result.get("intent", {}),
        citations=result.get("citations", []),
        confidence=result.get("confidence", 0.0),
        latencyms=latencyms,
    )
```


## ملاحظتان مهمتان

- لأن `/ask` في هذا الشكل يستخدم `get_current_user`، فهو endpoint محمي، وهذا متسق مع auth design في المرجع.[^48_1]
- إذا أردت `/ask` عامًا بدون login، ستحتاج optional auth dependency بدل `OAuth2PasswordBearer` الإجباري، وإلا سيُرفض الطلب بدون token.[^48_1]


## أين أصبحنا الآن

حتى هذه اللحظة صار عندك تقريبًا كامل العمود الفقري للنظام:[^48_2][^48_1]


| الطبقة | الحالة |
| :-- | :-- |
| Metadata DB + repositories | جاهزة مبدئيًا |
| Auth/JWT | جاهزة |
| Ingestion إلى Qdrant | جاهزة |
| Retrieval + filters | جاهزة |
| Reranking | جاهزة |
| Answer Agent | جاهز مبدئيًا |
| LangGraph orchestration | جاهز |
| QA endpoints | جاهزة |

## ما الناقص بعد ذلك

المرجع يلمّح إلى 3 تحسينات كبيرة بعد هذا المستوى:[^48_1]

- **Hybrid retrieval**: دمج metadata exact matching مع semantic retrieval بدل الاعتماد على vectors فقط.
- **Specialized agents**: مثل `QuranAgent`, `ZakatAgent`, وربما لاحقًا `HadithAgent` و`FiqhAgent`.
- **Production hardening**: caching، background jobs، Docker، monitoring، واختبارات unit/integration.

المرحلة التالية الأنسب الآن هي أن أكمل لك بـ:

1. `AuthorAgent`, `CategoryAgent`, `BookAgent`, `GUIDAgent` بشكل كامل، ثم
2. توصيل `QuranAgent` و`ZakatAgent` داخل graph routing، ثم
3. `docker-compose + requirements + .env.example`.

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^48_1]: chat-Islamic-RAG-Construction-1.txt

[^48_2]: README.md


---

# كمل

ممتاز، نكمل الآن بالـ **metadata agents المتخصصة** ثم نضيف `QuranAgent` و`ZakatAgent` وربطهم داخل graph، وبعدها أختم لك بملفات التشغيل الأساسية `requirements.txt` و`.env.example` و`docker-compose.yml`. هذا كله منسجم مع المرجع الذي يوصي بـ metadata agents مستقلة، وrouting لأنواع intents مثل `QURAN` و`ZAKAT`، مع تشغيل FastAPI وQdrant وPostgres في بيئة Docker عند الحاجة.[^49_1][^49_2]

## `app/agents/authoragent.py`

بما أن عندك حوالي `3,146` مؤلفًا، والـ `books.db` يدعم الربط عبر `bookauthors`، فالأفضل أن يبدأ AuthorAgent بـ exact/LIKE search بسيط وسريع على جدول `authors`.[^49_2][^49_1]

```python
from sqlalchemy import text
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

class AuthorAgent:
    def resolve(self, db: Session, query: str, intent: dict | None = None, limit: int = 10) -> list[dict]:
        rows = db.execute(text("""
            SELECT authorid, guid, shortid, name, death
            FROM authors
            WHERE name LIKE :q
            ORDER BY
                CASE WHEN name = :exact THEN 0 ELSE 1 END,
                LENGTH(name) ASC
            LIMIT :limit
        """), {
            "q": f"%{query.strip()}%",
            "exact": query.strip(),
            "limit": limit,
        }).mappings().all()

        return [dict(r) for r in rows]
```


## `app/agents/categoryagent.py`

التصنيفات عندك عددها `41` فقط، فـ category resolution يمكن أن يكون بسيطًا جدًا، ويعتمد على الاسم المباشر أو المطابقة الجزئية.[^49_1][^49_2]

```python
from sqlalchemy import text
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

class CategoryAgent:
    def resolve(self, db: Session, query: str, intent: dict | None = None, limit: int = 10) -> list[dict]:
        rows = db.execute(text("""
            SELECT catid, guid, name
            FROM categories
            WHERE name LIKE :q
            ORDER BY
                CASE WHEN name = :exact THEN 0 ELSE 1 END,
                LENGTH(name) ASC
            LIMIT :limit
        """), {
            "q": f"%{query.strip()}%",
            "exact": query.strip(),
            "limit": limit,
        }).mappings().all()

        return [dict(r) for r in rows]
```


## `app/agents/bookagent.py`

الـ BookAgent يجب أن يستفيد من author/category filters، ويعيد فقط الكتب المستخرجة افتراضيًا لأن corpus النصي الفعلي موجود عند الكتب المستخرجة تقريبًا كلها (`8,423` من `8,425`).[^49_2][^49_1]

```python
from sqlalchemy import text
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

class BookAgent:
    def find_books(
        self,
        db: Session,
        authorids: list[int] | None = None,
        categoryids: list[int] | None = None,
        intent: dict | None = None,
        limit: int = 50,
    ) -> list[dict]:
        authorids = authorids or []
        categoryids = categoryids or []

        sql = """
            SELECT DISTINCT b.bookid, b.guid, b.shortid, b.title, b.catid, b.catname, b.extracted, b.file, b.sizemb
            FROM books b
        """
        where = ["b.extracted = 1"]
        params = {"limit": limit}

        if authorids:
            sql += " JOIN bookauthors ba ON ba.bookid = b.bookid "
            placeholders = ",".join([f":a{i}" for i in range(len(authorids))])
            where.append(f"ba.authorid IN ({placeholders})")
            for i, aid in enumerate(authorids):
                params[f"a{i}"] = aid

        if categoryids:
            placeholders = ",".join([f":c{i}" for i in range(len(categoryids))])
            where.append(f"b.catid IN ({placeholders})")
            for i, cid in enumerate(categoryids):
                params[f"c{i}"] = cid

        sql += " WHERE " + " AND ".join(where)
        sql += " ORDER BY b.sizemb DESC NULLS LAST, b.bookid ASC LIMIT :limit"

        rows = db.execute(text(sql), params).mappings().all()
        return [dict(r) for r in rows]
```


## `app/agents/guidagent.py`

بما أن عندك GUID وshort ID كـ identifiers رسمية للكتاب، والـ README يوضح إمكانية البحث بهما مباشرة في `books.db` أو `guidindex.json`، فيكفي أن يبدأ GUIDAgent من `books.db` ثم يعمل fallback إلى repository لو أحببت لاحقًا.[^49_2]

```python
from sqlalchemy import text
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

class GUIDAgent:
    def resolve(self, db: Session, guid_or_shortid: str) -> dict | None:
        value = guid_or_shortid.strip()

        row = db.execute(text("""
            SELECT bookid, guid, shortid, title, catid, catname, extracted, file, sizemb
            FROM books
            WHERE guid = :value OR UPPER(shortid) = UPPER(:value)
            LIMIT 1
        """), {"value": value}).mappings().first()

        return dict(row) if row else None
```


## `app/agents/zakatagent.py`

المرجع يضع Zakat كمسار calculator لا يحتاج retrieval، ويستخدم قاعدة 2.5% مع nisab. هذه نسخة أولية جيدة جدًا للمسار الحسابي داخل graph.[^49_1]

```python
import re
from pydantic import BaseModel

class ZakatResult(BaseModel):
    totalwealth: float
    nisabthreshold: float
    zakatamount: float
    isabovenisab: bool
    message: str
    calculationmethod: str

class ZakatAgent:
    GOLD_PRICE_PER_GRAM = 250.0
    SILVER_PRICE_PER_GRAM = 3.0
    GOLD_NISAB_GRAMS = 85.0
    SILVER_NISAB_GRAMS = 595.0
    ZAKAT_RATE = 0.025

    def extract_amounts(self, query: str) -> list[float]:
        numbers = re.findall(r"\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?", query.replace(",", ""))
        return [float(n) for n in numbers]

    def calculate(self, query: str, intent: dict | None = None) -> dict:
        amounts = self.extract_amounts(query)
        if not amounts:
            return {
                "message": "لم يتم العثور على مبلغ واضح لحساب الزكاة.",
                "zakatamount": 0.0,
                "citations": [],
                "confidence": 0.9,
            }

        total = sum(amounts)
        gold_nisab = self.GOLD_NISAB_GRAMS * self.GOLD_PRICE_PER_GRAM
        silver_nisab = self.SILVER_NISAB_GRAMS * self.SILVER_PRICE_PER_GRAM
        nisab = min(gold_nisab, silver_nisab)

        above = total >= nisab
        zakat = total * self.ZAKAT_RATE if above else 0.0

        if above:
            message = f"الزكاة الواجبة تقريبًا هي {zakat:.2f}، على أساس 2.5% من إجمالي {total:.2f}."
        else:
            message = f"المبلغ أقل من النصاب التقديري {nisab:.2f}، فلا زكاة واجبة في هذا الحساب المبسط."

        return {
            "message": message,
            "zakatamount": zakat,
            "citations": [],
            "confidence": 0.95,
            "details": {
                "totalwealth": total,
                "nisabthreshold": nisab,
                "isabovenisab": above,
                "calculationmethod": "2.5% simplified estimation",
            }
        }
```


## `app/agents/quranagent.py`

المرجع يتعامل مع `QuranAgent` كوكيل متخصص في الآيات، مع استخراج مرجع سورة/آية لو وجد. في البداية لا نحتاج محرك قرآن منفصل؛ يكفي أن يعالج chunks المسترجعة ويعطي جوابًا منظمًا.[^49_1]

```python
import re
from typing import List, Dict, Any

class QuranAgent:
    def extract_verse_reference(self, query: str) -> dict | None:
        match = re.search(r"(\d+)\s*[:/]\s*(\d+)", query)
        if match:
            return {
                "surah": int(match.group(1)),
                "ayah": int(match.group(2)),
            }
        return None

    def process(self, query: str, chunks: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> dict:
        verse_ref = self.extract_verse_reference(query)

        if not chunks:
            return {
                "answer": "لم يتم العثور على سياق قرآني كافٍ للإجابة.",
                "citations": [],
                "confidence": 0.2,
                "versereference": verse_ref,
            }

        top = chunks[:5]
        lines = []
        for i, chunk in enumerate(top, start=1):
            lines.append(f"[C{i}] {chunk.get('booktitle', 'مصدر غير معروف')}: {chunk.get('text', '')[:350]}")

        answer = "إجابة قرآنية أولية مبنية على المقاطع المسترجعة:\n\n" + "\n\n".join(lines)

        citations = []
        for chunk in top:
            citations.append({
                "bookid": chunk.get("bookid"),
                "booktitle": chunk.get("booktitle", ""),
                "bookguid": chunk.get("bookguid", ""),
                "chunkid": chunk.get("chunkid", ""),
                "chunkindex": chunk.get("chunkindex", 0),
                "text": chunk.get("text", "")[:280],
                "relevancescore": chunk.get("rerankscore", chunk.get("score", 0.0)),
            })

        return {
            "answer": answer,
            "citations": citations,
            "confidence": 0.85,
            "versereference": verse_ref,
        }
```


## تعديل `app/graph/nodes.py` للمسارات المتخصصة

المرجع يقترح أن `answernode` يقرر بين `ZAKAT`, `QURAN`, وgeneral answer generation بحسب intent.[^49_1]
لذلك عدّل `answer_node` ليصبح هكذا:

```python
from app.agents.zakatagent import ZakatAgent
from app.agents.quranagent import QuranAgent

zakat_agent = ZakatAgent()
quran_agent = QuranAgent()

def answer_node(state, llm=None):
    query = state["query"]
    intent = state.get("intent", {})
    intent_type = intent.get("intent", "ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE")
    chunks = state.get("rerankedchunks") or state.get("retrievalchunks") or []

    if intent_type == "ZAKAT":
        result = zakat_agent.calculate(query=query, intent=intent)
        return {
            "answer": result["message"],
            "citations": result.get("citations", []),
            "confidence": result.get("confidence", 0.95),
        }

    if intent_type == "QURAN":
        result = quran_agent.process(query=query, chunks=chunks)
        return {
            "answer": result["answer"],
            "citations": result["citations"],
            "confidence": result["confidence"],
        }

    answer_agent = AnswerAgent(llm=llm)
    result = answer_agent.generate(query=query, chunks=chunks, intent=intent)

    return {
        "answer": result.answer,
        "citations": result.citations,
        "confidence": result.confidence,
    }
```


## تحسين صغير في `builder.py`

لو أردت أن تقلل المرور غير الضروري على retrieval في مسارات مثل `ZAKAT`, يمكن جعل graph يذهب مباشرة إلى `answer` عندما `requiresretrieval=False`. هذا منسجم مع idea الـ calculators/tool intents في المرجع.[^49_1]

```python
def route_decision(state) -> Literal["guid", "author", "plan"]:
    intent = state.get("intent", {})
    entities = intent.get("entities", {})

    if entities.get("guid") or entities.get("shortid"):
        return "guid"

    if intent.get("requiresretrieval", False):
        return "author"

    return "plan"

def plan_decision(state) -> Literal["retrieve", "answer"]:
    plan = state.get("retrievalplan", {})
    if plan.get("mode") == "metadataonly":
        return "answer"
    return "retrieve"

graph.add_conditional_edges(
    "plan",
    plan_decision,
    {
        "retrieve": "retrieve",
        "answer": "answer",
    },
)
```

وفي هذه الحالة احذف:

```python
graph.add_edge("plan", "retrieve")
```

وأبقِ:

```python
graph.add_edge("retrieve", "rerank")
graph.add_edge("rerank", "answer")
```

## تعديل `app/core/config.py`

حتى تشتغل الأسماء السابقة، تأكد أن config يستخدم نفس المفاتيح.[^49_1]

```python
from typing import Optional, List
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    APPNAME: str = "Islamic RAG System"
    APPVERSION: str = "1.0.0"
    DEBUG: bool = True

    DATABASEURL: str = "sqlite:///./data/metadata/books.db"

    SECRETKEY: str = "change-me"
    ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    ACCESSTOKENEXPIREMINUTES: int = 30

    QDRANTURL: str = "http://localhost:6333"
    QDRANTAPIKEY: Optional[str] = None

    EMBEDDINGMODEL: str = "BAAI/bge-m3"
    RERANKERMODEL: str = "BAAI/bge-reranker-v2-m3"
    LLMMODEL: str = "Qwen/Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct"

    TOPK: int = 10
    RERANKTOPK: int = 5
    SIMILARITYTHRESHOLD: float = 0.7

    CHUNKSIZE: int = 1200
    CHUNKOVERLAP: int = 150
    CONFIDENCETHRESHOLD: float = 0.7

    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
        case_sensitive = True

settings = Settings()
```

```yaml
    build: .
    container_name: islamic-rag-app
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    environment:
      - DATABASEURL=sqlite:///./data/metadata/books.db
      - QDRANTURL=http://qdrant:6333
      - SECRETKEY=change-this-secret

      - ./:/app
    depends_on:
      - qdrant

  qdrant:
    image: qdrant/qdrant:latest
    container_name: islamic-rag-qdrant
    ports:
      - "6333:6333"
    volumes:
      - qdrant_data:/qdrant/storage

volumes:
  qdrant_data:
```

## أين وصل النظام الآن

الآن صار عندك هيكل شبه كامل من ناحية التنفيذ:[^49_2][^49_1]


| الجزء | الحالة |
| :-- | :-- |
| Metadata DB | جاهز |
| Metadata Agents | جاهزة |
| GUID / short ID resolution | جاهز |
| Ingestion to Qdrant | جاهز |
| Retrieval + Filters | جاهز |
| Reranking | جاهز |
| Quran / Zakat specialized routes | جاهزة أوليًا |
| LangGraph orchestration | جاهز |
| Auth + QA API | جاهز |
| Docker + env + requirements | جاهز |

## ما الذي يبقى فعليًا

المرحلـة التالية بعد هذا ليست “بناء معماري” بقدر ما هي **hardening وتخصيص domain**:[^49_1]

- `RouterAgent` يحتاج prompt/classification أدق للتمييز بين `QURAN`, `FIQH`, `DUA`, و`GENERAL`.
- `QuranAgent` يحتاج لاحقًا index خاص بالمصحف أو corpus verse-level بدل الاعتماد فقط على chunks العامة.
- `AnswerAgent` يحتاج LLM حقيقي موصول، مع prompt citations صارم.
- `AuthorAgent` و`CategoryAgent` يستفيدون لاحقًا من normalization عربي أفضل، مثل إزالة "الـ" والتشكيل وتوحيد الهمزات.

أفضل خطوة تالية الآن هي أن أحوّل كل هذا إلى **project tree نهائي جاهز للنسخ** مع ملفات كاملة مرتبة file-by-file، أو أن أبني لك **نسخة MVP runnable** مضغوطة في ملف واحد/عدة ملفات جاهزة.

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^49_1]: chat-Islamic-RAG-Construction-1.txt

[^49_2]: README.md


---

# كمل المرحله التاليه

المرحلة التالية الآن ليست إضافة agents جديدة، بل **تحويل النظام من prototype إلى MVP مضبوط**: Router أقوى، hybrid retrieval، citation validation، monitoring، وtests. المرجع نفسه يركز بعد المعمارية الأساسية على هذه الطبقات: classifier متدرج، hybrid search، response validation، logging، واختبارات تقييم للـ intents والاسترجاع.[^50_1]

## ما نبنيه الآن

سنكمل هذه الأجزاء بالترتيب:[^50_1]

- **RouterAgent أقوى**: special patterns + LLM + embedding fallback.
- **Arabic normalization**: قبل classification والبحث.
- **Hybrid retrieval**: vector + metadata + BM25/keyword.
- **Citation validator**: يمنع hallucinated citations.
- **Monitoring + tests**: لقياس intent accuracy وretrieval quality.
هذا هو الفرق بين “كود شغال” و“نظام يمكن الوثوق به”.[^50_1]


## `app/services/normalizer.py`

بما أن corpus عربي، فالـ normalization مهم جدًا لتحسين author/category matching والـ retrieval عمومًا، خصوصًا مع الهمزات والتشكيل وتنوّع كتابة الألف والياء.[^50_1]

```python
import re

class ArabicNormalizer:
    TATWEEL = "ـ"
    DIACRITICS_PATTERN = re.compile(r"[\u064B-\u065F\u0670\u06D6-\u06ED]")
    WHITESPACE_PATTERN = re.compile(r"\s+")

    def normalize(self, text: str) -> str:
        if not text:
            return ""

        text = text.strip()
        text = text.replace("أ", "ا").replace("إ", "ا").replace("آ", "ا")
        text = text.replace("ى", "ي")
        text = text.replace("ؤ", "و").replace("ئ", "ي")
        text = text.replace("ة", "ه")
        text = text.replace(self.TATWEEL, "")
        text = self.DIACRITICS_PATTERN.sub("", text)
        text = self.WHITESPACE_PATTERN.sub(" ", text)
        return text.lower()

    def normalize_for_match(self, text: str) -> str:
        text = self.normalize(text)
        text = re.sub(r"[^\w\s]", " ", text)
        text = self.WHITESPACE_PATTERN.sub(" ", text)
        return text.strip()
```


## `app/agents/router.py`

المرجع يقترح router متدرج:

1) special patterns مثل GUID وshort ID،
2) LLM classification،
3) embedding fallback إذا كانت الثقة ضعيفة.[^50_1]
```python
import json
import re
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer

from app.core.config import settings
from app.services.normalizer import ArabicNormalizer

class UserIntent(BaseModel):
    intent: str = Field(description="FIQH, QURAN, ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE, GREETING, ZAKAT, INHERITANCE, DUA, HIJRICALENDAR, PRAYERTIMES")
    confidence: float
    language: str
    requiresretrieval: bool
    subintent: Optional[str] = None
    entities: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    reasoning: str
    nextaction: str

class RouterAgent:
    GUIDPATTERN = re.compile(r"\b[a-f0-9]{8}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{12}\b", re.I)
    SHORTIDPATTERN = re.compile(r"\b[A-F0-9]{6}\b", re.I)
    NUMBERPATTERN = re.compile(r"\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?")

    EXAMPLES = {
        "FIQH": ["ما حكم بيع الدين", "حكم التورق", "ما حكم صلاة الجماعة", "هل هذا جائز شرعا"],
        "QURAN": ["فسر آية", "ما معنى هذه الآية", "البقرة 255", "آية الكرسي"],
        "ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE": ["من هو ابن تيمية", "ما معنى الإحسان", "ما تعريف السنة"],
        "GREETING": ["السلام عليكم", "مرحبا", "اهلا"],
        "ZAKAT": ["احسب زكاة 10000", "عندي 250000 كم الزكاة", "زكاة المال"],
        "INHERITANCE": ["قسمة الميراث", "توفي رجل وترك زوجة وابنا", "حساب المواريث"],
        "DUA": ["دعاء السفر", "دعاء الكرب", "اذكار النوم"],
        "HIJRICALENDAR": ["ما التاريخ الهجري", "كم اليوم هجري"],
        "PRAYERTIMES": ["متى صلاة المغرب", "موعد الفجر", "مواقيت الصلاة"],
    }

    def __init__(self, llm=None):
        self.llm = llm
        self.normalizer = ArabicNormalizer()
        self.embeddingmodel = SentenceTransformer(settings.EMBEDDINGMODEL)
        self.intent_embeddings = self._build_intent_embeddings()

    def _build_intent_embeddings(self):
        result = {}
        for intent, examples in self.EXAMPLES.items():
            emb = self.embeddingmodel.encode(examples, normalize_embeddings=True)
            result[intent] = emb.mean(axis=0)
        return result

    def classify(self, query: str) -> UserIntent:
        query = query.strip()

        special = self._check_special_patterns(query)
        if special:
            return special

        llm_result = self._llm_classify(query)
        if llm_result and llm_result.confidence >= settings.CONFIDENCETHRESHOLD:
            return llm_result

        return self._embedding_fallback(query)

    def _check_special_patterns(self, query: str) -> Optional[UserIntent]:
        guid_match = self.GUIDPATTERN.search(query)
        if guid_match:
            return UserIntent(
                intent="ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE",
                confidence=0.95,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=True,
                subintent="GUIDLOOKUP",
                entities={"guid": guid_match.group(0)},
                reasoning="GUID detected in query",
                nextaction="metadataonly",
            )

        short_match = self.SHORTIDPATTERN.search(query)
        if short_match:
            return UserIntent(
                intent="ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE",
                confidence=0.90,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=True,
                subintent="SHORTIDLOOKUP",
                entities={"shortid": short_match.group(0).upper()},
                reasoning="Short ID detected in query",
                nextaction="metadataonly",
            )

        normalized = self.normalizer.normalize_for_match(query)

        if "زكاه" in normalized or "زكاة" in query:
            numbers = self.NUMBERPATTERN.findall(query)
            return UserIntent(
                intent="ZAKAT",
                confidence=0.92 if numbers else 0.75,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=False,
                entities={"amounts": [float(n.replace(",", "")) for n in numbers]} if numbers else {},
                reasoning="Zakat intent detected",
                nextaction="calculator",
            )

        if any(kw in normalized for kw in ["ميراث", "مواريث", "ورث", "ارث"]):
            return UserIntent(
                intent="INHERITANCE",
                confidence=0.90,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=False,
                reasoning="Inheritance intent detected",
                nextaction="calculator",
            )

        if any(kw in normalized for kw in ["هجري", "التاريخ الهجري"]):
            return UserIntent(
                intent="HIJRICALENDAR",
                confidence=0.88,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=False,
                reasoning="Hijri calendar intent detected",
                nextaction="tool",
            )

        if any(kw in normalized for kw in ["الفجر", "الظهر", "العصر", "المغرب", "العشاء", "مواقيت", "الصلاه", "الصلاة"]):
            return UserIntent(
                intent="PRAYERTIMES",
                confidence=0.85,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=False,
                reasoning="Prayer times intent detected",
                nextaction="tool",
            )
```
