## 4) `app/models/agentstate.py`

هذا الملف يحدد GraphState الذي يستخدمه LangGraph.[^62_1]

```python
# app/models/agentstate.py
from typing import TypedDict, List, Dict, Any, Optional


class GraphState(TypedDict, total=False):
    # Input
    query: str
    userid: Optional[int]

    # Classification
    intent: Dict[str, Any]
    normalizedquery: str

    # Metadata agents outputs
    authorcandidates: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    categorycandidates: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    bookcandidates: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    guidcandidate: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]

    # Retrieval
    retrievalplan: Dict[str, Any]
    retrievalchunks: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    rerankedchunks: List[Dict[str, Any]]

    # Answer
    evidence: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    answer: str
    citations: List[Dict[str, Any]]

    # Meta
    latencyms: float
    confidence: float
    error: Optional[str]
```

هذا مطابق تقريبًا لتعريف GraphState في النص عندك.[^62_1]

***

## 5) Repositories

نأتي الآن لطبقة الـ repositories التي تجعل API نظيفة وتسهّل استخدام metadata قبل RAG.
المراجع عندك تشير إلى `BookRepository`, `AuthorRepository`, `CategoryRepository`.[^62_1]

### `app/repositories/books.py`

```python
# app/repositories/books.py
from typing import List, Optional
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from sqlalchemy import select
from app.models.dbmodels import Book, Author


class BookRepository:
    def __init__(self, db: Session):
        self.db = db

    def get_by_id(self, bookid: int) -> Optional[Book]:
        return self.db.get(Book, bookid)

    def get_by_guid(self, guid: str) -> Optional[Book]:
        stmt = select(Book).where(Book.guid == guid)
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().first()

    def get_by_shortid(self, shortid: str) -> Optional[Book]:
        stmt = select(Book).where(Book.shortid == shortid)
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().first()

    def search(
        self,
        query: Optional[str] = None,
        catid: Optional[int] = None,
        authorid: Optional[int] = None,
        extracted: Optional[bool] = None,
        skip: int = 0,
        limit: int = 20,
    ) -> List[Book]:
        stmt = select(Book)

        if query:
            like = f"%{query}%"
            stmt = stmt.where(Book.title.ilike(like))

        if catid is not None:
            stmt = stmt.where(Book.catid == catid)

        if extracted is not None:
            stmt = stmt.where(Book.extracted == extracted)

        if authorid is not None:
            stmt = (
                stmt.join(Book.authors)
                .where(Author.authorid == authorid)
                .distinct()
            )

        stmt = stmt.order_by(Book.title).offset(skip).limit(limit)
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()

    def get_by_category(self, catid: int) -> List[Book]:
        stmt = select(Book).where(Book.catid == catid, Book.extracted == True)
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()

    def get_by_author(self, authorid: int) -> List[Book]:
        stmt = (
            select(Book)
            .join(Book.authors)
            .where(Author.authorid == authorid, Book.extracted == True)
        )
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()
```


### `app/repositories/authors.py`

```python
# app/repositories/authors.py
from typing import List, Optional
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from sqlalchemy import select
from app.models.dbmodels import Author


class AuthorRepository:
    def __init__(self, db: Session):
        self.db = db

    def get_by_id(self, authorid: int) -> Optional[Author]:
        return self.db.get(Author, authorid)

    def get_by_guid(self, guid: str) -> Optional[Author]:
        stmt = select(Author).where(Author.guid == guid)
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().first()

    def search(self, q: Optional[str] = None, skip: int = 0, limit: int = 50) -> List[Author]:
        stmt = select(Author)
        if q:
            like = f"%{q}%"
            stmt = stmt.where(Author.name.ilike(like))
        stmt = stmt.order_by(Author.name).offset(skip).limit(limit)
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()

    def list_all(self, limit: int = 1000) -> List[Author]:
        stmt = select(Author).order_by(Author.name).limit(limit)
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()
```


### `app/repositories/categories.py`

```python
# app/repositories/categories.py
from typing import List, Optional
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from sqlalchemy import select
from app.models.dbmodels import Category, Book


class CategoryRepository:
    def __init__(self, db: Session):
        self.db = db

    def get_by_id(self, catid: int) -> Optional[Category]:
        return self.db.get(Category, catid)

    def list_all(self) -> List[Category]:
        stmt = select(Category).order_by(Category.catid)
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()

    def get_books(self, catid: int) -> List[Book]:
        stmt = (
            select(Book)
            .where(Book.catid == catid, Book.extracted == True)
            .order_by(Book.title)
        )
        return self.db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()
```


### `app/repositories/guidindex.py` (اختياري لكن مفيد)

يمكنك لاحقًا استخدام `guid_index.json` مباشرة، لكن وجود repository ل GUID يعطيك abstraction أفضل.[^62_2][^62_1]

```python
# app/repositories/guidindex.py
import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from app.core.config import settings


class GUIDIndexRepository:
    def __init__(self, path: Optional[Path] = None):
        self.path = path or Path(settings.METADATA_DIR) / "guidindex.json"
        self._index = None

    def load(self):
        if self._index is None:
            with open(self.path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                self._index = json.load(f)
        return self._index

    def get_book_by_guid(self, guid: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = self.load()
        return data.get("guids", {}).get(guid)
```

README يؤكد وجود `guidindex.json` بهذا الشكل تقريبًا.[^62_2]

***

## 6) API بسيطة للـ metadata

الآن يمكنك إضافة APIs مبكرة كما في مرجعك، قبل الدخول في agents وRAG.[^62_1]

### `app/api/books.py`

```python
# app/api/books.py
from typing import List, Optional
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import get_db
from app.models.schemas import BookResponse
from app.repositories.books import BookRepository

router = APIRouter(prefix="/books", tags=["books"])


@router.get("/search", response_model=List[BookResponse])
def search_books(
    q: Optional[str] = None,
    catid: Optional[int] = None,
    authorid: Optional[int] = None,
    extracted: Optional[bool] = None,
    skip: int = 0,
    limit: int = 20,
    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
):
    repo = BookRepository(db)
    books = repo.search(
        query=q,
        catid=catid,
        authorid=authorid,
        extracted=extracted,
        skip=skip,
        limit=limit,
    )
    return books


@router.get("/{bookid}", response_model=BookResponse)
def get_book(bookid: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    repo = BookRepository(db)
    book = repo.get_by_id(bookid)
    if not book:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="Book not found"
        )
    return book


@router.get("/guid/{guid}", response_model=BookResponse)
def get_book_by_guid(guid: str, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    repo = BookRepository(db)
    book = repo.get_by_guid(guid)
    if not book:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="Book not found"
        )
    return book
```


### `app/api/authors.py`

```python
# app/api/authors.py
from typing import List, Optional
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import get_db
from app.models.schemas import AuthorResponse
from app.repositories.authors import AuthorRepository

router = APIRouter(prefix="/authors", tags=["authors"])


@router.get("", response_model=List[AuthorResponse])
def list_authors(
    q: Optional[str] = None,
    skip: int = 0,
    limit: int = 100,
    db: Session = Depends(get_db),
):
    repo = AuthorRepository(db)
    if q:
        return repo.search(q=q, skip=skip, limit=limit)
    return repo.list_all(limit=limit)


@router.get("/{authorid}", response_model=AuthorResponse)
def get_author(authorid: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    repo = AuthorRepository(db)
    author = repo.get_by_id(authorid)
    return author
```


### `app/api/categories.py`

```python
# app/api/categories.py
from typing import List
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import get_db
from app.models.schemas import CategoryResponse, BookResponse
from app.repositories.categories import CategoryRepository

router = APIRouter(prefix="/categories", tags=["categories"])


@router.get("", response_model=List[CategoryResponse])
def list_categories(db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    repo = CategoryRepository(db)
    return repo.list_all()


@router.get("/{catid}", response_model=CategoryResponse)
def get_category(catid: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    repo = CategoryRepository(db)
    category = repo.get_by_id(catid)
    return category


@router.get("/{catid}/books", response_model=List[BookResponse])
def get_category_books(catid: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    repo = CategoryRepository(db)
    return repo.get_books(catid)
```

## 7) `app/main.py`

أخيرًا اربط كل شيء مع FastAPI كما في تصميمك.[^62_1]

```python
# app/main.py
from datetime import datetime
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

from app.core.config import settings
from app.core.db import Base, engine
from app.api import books, authors, categories  # لاحقًا: qa, auth, admin


Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)

app = FastAPI(
    title=settings.APPNAME,
    version=settings.APPVERSION,
    description="Islamic RAG System based on Shamela metadata and grounded QA architecture.",
)

app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],  # عدّلها لاحقًا للإنتاج
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)


app.include_router(books.router)
app.include_router(authors.router)
app.include_router(categories.router)


@app.get("/")
def root():
    return {
        "name": settings.APPNAME,
        "version": settings.APPVERSION,
        "docs": "/docs",
    }


@app.get("/health")
def healthcheck():
    return {"status": "healthy", "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}
```

بعد إضافة هذه الملفات وتشغيل:

```bash

```

تستطيع فعليًا:

- استعلام `/books/search?q=...`
- استعلام `/authors?q=...`
- استعلام `/categories` و`/categories/{catid}/books`

هذه الطبقة هي قاعدة السلم لكل ما سيأتي: vector index, retrieval planner, router agent, LangGraph, SQL agent، إلخ.[^62_1]

لو حابب، الخطوة التالية بالتفصيل أقدر أبني لك:

- `app/ingestion/loadsqlite.py` و `build_vector_index.py` مكتملين مع `Chunk` table بدلاً من فقط Qdrant، أو
- ننتقل مباشرة لـ `RouterAgent` + LangGraph nodes كما كانت الخطة في الملف المرجعي.

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^62_1]: chat-Islamic-RAG-Construction-1.txt

[^62_2]: README.md

# كمل بالتفصيل

نكمل الآن بطبقة **ingestion + vector index + retrieval service**؛ هذه التي تربط الكتب الفعلية بالـ vector DB وتجهّز الأرضية لـ Router وLangGraph.[^63_1]

***

## 1) `app/ingestion/loadsqlite.py` (نسخة منسجمة مع الـ schema)

بما أنك بالفعل عندك تعريفات الجداول وملف metadata في المرجع، نضبط السكربت على ذلك.[^63_2][^63_1]

```python
# app/ingestion/loadsqlite.py
from pathlib import Path
import json
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import Base, engine, SessionLocal
from app.core.config import settings
from app.models.dbmodels import Book, Author, Category, bookauthors


def _load_json(path: Path):
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return json.load(f)


def load_categories(db: Session, path: Path):
    data = _load_json(path)
    items = data.get("categories", data)

    for cat in items:
        row = Category(
            catid=cat.get("id") or cat.get("catid"),
            guid=cat["guid"],
            name=cat["name"],
        )
        db.merge(row)

    db.commit()
    print(f"Loaded {len(items)} categories from {path}")


def load_authors(db: Session, path: Path):
    data = _load_json(path)
    items = data.get("authors", data)

    for author in items:
        row = Author(
            authorid=author.get("id") or author.get("authorid"),
            guid=author["guid"],
            shortid=author.get("shortid", ""),
            name=author["name"],
            death=author.get("death"),
        )
        db.merge(row)

    db.commit()
    print(f"Loaded {len(items)} authors from {path}")


def load_books(db: Session, path: Path):
    data = _load_json(path)
    items = data.get("books", data)

    for book in items:
        b = Book(
            bookid=book.get("id") or book.get("bookid"),
            guid=book["guid"],
            shortid=book.get("shortid", ""),
            title=book["title"],
            catid=book.get("catid"),
            catname=book.get("catname", ""),
            date=str(book.get("date") or ""),
            authorstr=book.get("authorstr", ""),
            extracted=bool(book.get("extracted", False)),
            file=book.get("file"),
            sizemb=float(book.get("sizemb") or 0),
            language="ar",
            verified=False,
        )
        db.merge(b)
        db.flush()

        for a in book.get("authors", []):
            authorid = a.get("id") or a.get("authorid")
            stmt = bookauthors.insert().values(
                bookid=b.bookid,
                authorid=authorid,
                guid=a.get("guid"),
                role=a.get("role", "main"),
            )
            # SQLite-only ignore duplicates
            try:
                db.execute(stmt)
            except Exception:
                db.rollback()

    db.commit()
    print(f"Loaded {len(items)} books from {path}")


def main():
    Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)
    db = SessionLocal()
    try:
        meta_dir = Path(settings.METADATA_DIR)
        load_categories(db, meta_dir / "categories.json")
        load_authors(db, meta_dir / "authors.json")
        load_books(db, meta_dir / "books.json")
        print("SQLite metadata load completed.")
    finally:
        db.close()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

البيانات في README والملف المرجعي تؤكد أن `books.json`, `authors.json`, `categories.json` لها الحقول المستخدمة هنا.[^63_1][^63_2]

***

## 2) `app/ingestion/chunkprocessor.py`

استخدام `RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter` كما في المرجع، مع chunk size 512 وoverlap 50.[^63_1]

```python
# app/ingestion/chunkprocessor.py
from langchain.text_splitter import RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter


def chunk_text(text: str, chunk_size: int, chunk_overlap: int) -> list[str]:
    splitter = RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(
        chunk_size=chunk_size,
        chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap,
        separators=["\n\n", "\n", "۔", ".", " ", ""],
    )
    chunks = splitter.split_text(text)
    return [c.strip() for c in chunks if c.strip()]
```


***

## 3) `app/services/vectorstore.py` (Qdrant)

المرجع عندك يتحدث عن استخدام Qdrant مع bge-m3 أو Qwen Embedding، وQdrant هو اختيار قوي مذكور في كتاب الـ LLM Handbook كذلك.[^63_3][^63_1]

```python
# app/services/vectorstore.py
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional

from qdrant_client import QdrantClient
from qdrant_client.models import Distance, VectorParams, PointStruct, Filter, FieldCondition, MatchValue
from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer

from app.core.config import settings


class QdrantVectorStore:
    def __init__(self):
        self.client = QdrantClient(
            url=settings.QDRANTURL,
            api_key=settings.QDRANTAPIKEY or None,
        )
        self.collection_name = settings.QDRANTCOLLECTION
        self.embedding_model = SentenceTransformer(settings.EMBEDDINGMODEL)

    def _embedding_dim(self) -> int:
        vec = self.embedding_model.encode("السلام عليكم")
        return len(vec)

    def ensure_collection(self):
        collections = [c.name for c in self.client.get_collections().collections]
        if self.collection_name in collections:
            return

        self.client.create_collection(
            collection_name=self.collection_name,
            vectors_config=VectorParams(
                size=self._embedding_dim(),
                distance=Distance.COSINE,
            ),
        )

    def add_chunks(self, chunks: List[Dict[str, Any]]):
        texts = [c["text"] for c in chunks]
        vectors = self.embedding_model.encode(texts).tolist()

        points = []
        for chunk, vec in zip(chunks, vectors):
            pid = abs(hash(f'{chunk["bookid"]}-{chunk["chunkindex"]}'))
            points.append(
                PointStruct(
                    id=pid,
                    vector=vec,
                    payload=chunk,
                )
            )

        self.client.upsert(collection_name=self.collection_name, points=points)

    def search(
        self,
        query: str,
        k: int,
        filter_dict: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        query_vec = self.embedding_model.encode(query).tolist()
        qfilter = None
        if filter_dict:
            conditions = []
            for key, value in filter_dict.items():
                if isinstance(value, list):
                    conditions.append(FieldCondition(key=key, match=MatchValue(value=value)))
                else:
                    conditions.append(FieldCondition(key=key, match=MatchValue(value=value)))
            qfilter = Filter(must=conditions)

        result = self.client.search(
            collection_name=self.collection_name,
            query_vector=query_vec,
            limit=k,
            query_filter=qfilter,
        )

        formatted = []
        for r in result:
            payload = dict(r.payload)
            payload["score"] = float(r.score)
            formatted.append(payload)
        return formatted
```

هذا يتماشى مع تصميمك الذي يستخدم Qdrant + BGE-M3 لهذا المشروع.[^63_1]

***

## 4) `app/ingestion/build_vector_index.py`

هذا السكربت يقرأ كتبًا مستخرجة من `data/extractedbooks`, يعثر على metadata من Book، يقطع النص، ثم يرفع إلى Qdrant.[^63_2][^63_1]

```python
# app/ingestion/build_vector_index.py
from pathlib import Path
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import SessionLocal
from app.core.config import settings
from app.models.dbmodels import Book
from app.ingestion.chunkprocessor import chunk_text
from app.services.vectorstore import QdrantVectorStore


def iter_chunks(db: Session):
    extracted_dir = Path(settings.EXTRACTEDBOOKS_DIR)
    books = (
        db.query(Book)
        .filter(Book.extracted == True)
        .order_by(Book.catid, Book.bookid)
        .all()
    )

    for book in books:
        if not book.file:
            continue
        file_path = extracted_dir / book.file
        if not file_path.exists():
            continue

        try:
            text = file_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
        except Exception:
            continue

        chunks = chunk_text(
            text=text,
            chunk_size=settings.CHUNKSIZE,
            chunk_overlap=settings.CHUNKOVERLAP,
        )

        for idx, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
            yield {
                "bookid": book.bookid,
                "bookguid": book.guid,
                "booktitle": book.title,
                "categoryid": book.catid,
                "categoryname": book.catname,
                "chunkindex": idx,
                "text": chunk,
                "textlen": len(chunk),
                "sourcefile": book.file,
            }


def main():
    db = SessionLocal()
    try:
        vs = QdrantVectorStore()
        vs.ensure_collection()

        batch = []
        for item in iter_chunks(db):
            batch.append(item)
            if len(batch) >= 100:
                vs.add_chunks(batch)
                batch = []

        if batch:
            vs.add_chunks(batch)

        print("Vector index build completed.")
    finally:
        db.close()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

## 6) طبقة retrieval service (خارج LangGraph مؤقتًا)

قبل بناء LangGraph، الأفضل أن تملك خدمة retrieval واضحة تستخدم Qdrant + filters.
المرجع عندك يطرح `RetrievalPlanner` + `ChunkRetriever`.[^63_1]

### `app/services/retrieval.py`

```python
# app/services/retrieval.py
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.config import settings
from app.models.dbmodels import Book
from app.services.vectorstore import QdrantVectorStore


class RetrievalPlanner:
    def __init__(self, db: Session):
        self.db = db

    def create_plan(self, intent: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        entities = intent.get("entities", {})
        bookids = entities.get("bookids") or []
        categoryids = entities.get("categoryids") or []
        authorids = entities.get("authorids") or []

        mode = "rag" if intent.get("requiresretrieval", True) else "metadataonly"

        return {
            "mode": mode,
            "bookids": bookids,
            "categoryids": categoryids,
            "authorids": authorids,
            "extractedonly": True,
            "intent": intent.get("intent"),
        }

    def get_candidate_books(self, plan: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Book]:
        query = self.db.query(Book)
        if plan.get("extractedonly", True):
            query = query.filter(Book.extracted == True)

        if plan.get("categoryids"):
            query = query.filter(Book.catid.in_(plan["categoryids"]))

        if plan.get("bookids"):
            query = query.filter(Book.bookid.in_(plan["bookids"]))

        # لو authorids موجودة نحتاج join على authors (ممكن تأجّلها أو تضيف join)
        return query.all()


class RetrievalService:
    def __init__(self, vectorstore: Optional[QdrantVectorStore] = None):
        self.vectorstore = vectorstore or QdrantVectorStore()

    def search(
        self,
        query: str,
        plan: Dict[str, Any],
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        if plan.get("mode") == "metadataonly":
            return []

        filter_dict = {}
        if plan.get("bookids"):
            filter_dict["bookid"] = plan["bookids"]
        if plan.get("categoryids"):
            filter_dict["categoryid"] = plan["categoryids"]

        k = settings.TOPK
        results = self.vectorstore.search(query=query, k=k, filter_dict=filter_dict or None)
        return results
```

هذا يغطي فكرة **hierarchical retrieval** في المرجع:
أولًا تضيق على مستوى books (بناءً على intent/metadata)، ثم تبحث في chunks فقط ضمن هذا subset، لا corpus كله.[^63_1]

***

## 7) أول اختبار يدوي مفيد

بعد كل ما سبق، يمكنك تشغيل:

```bash
poetry poe load-sqlite
poetry poe build-index
poetry poe dev
```

ثم:

- اختبار `/books/search?q=...`
- ثم تجربة retrieval يدويًا داخل سكربت صغير (حتى قبل LangGraph) مثل:

```python
# scratch_retrieval.py (للاختبار فقط)
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from app.core.db import SessionLocal
from app.services.retrieval import RetrievalPlanner, RetrievalService

db: Session = SessionLocal()
planner = RetrievalPlanner(db)
retriever = RetrievalService()

intent = {
    "intent": "FIQH",
    "requiresretrieval": True,
    "entities": {"categoryids": [^63_1]},  # مثال
}
plan = planner.create_plan(intent)
chunks = retriever.search("حكم بيع العينة", plan)
print(len(chunks), "chunks")
print(chunks[^63_0]["booktitle"], chunks[^63_0]["text"][:300])
```

هذا يضمن أن:

- الـ metadata موجودة.
- الـ chunks في Qdrant.
- retrieval يعمل بالفلترة.

***

## ما الجاهز الآن قبل الدخول في agents وLangGraph

- طبقة DB + models + repositories.[^63_1]
- ingestion من JSON إلى SQLite.[^63_2][^63_1]
- chunking + vector index في Qdrant.[^63_1]
- retrieval service حقيقي يستخدم metadata filters.[^63_1]

هذه بالضبط هي الطبقة التي يصر عليها المرجع قبل أي شيء Agentic أو LangGraph، لأنها تجعل RAG **grounded** في الهيكل الصحيح للبيانات، لا مجرد vector search عشوائي.[^63_1]

السؤال الآن:
هل تحب أن أكمل بالتفصيل في الخطوة التالية مع **RouterAgent + المؤشرات (entities) + LangGraph nodes**، أم تفضل أن نبني أولًا **AnswerAgent + prompts + citation validation** قبل orchestration؟

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^63_1]: chat-Islamic-RAG-Construction-1.txt

[^63_2]: README.md

[^63_3]: LLM_Engineers_Handbook_Master_the_art_of_engineering_large_language-54-83.pdf


---

# كمل بالتفصيل

نكمل الآن بطبقة **RouterAgent + LangGraph nodes الأساسية**؛ هذه التي تحول السؤال إلى intent + خطة retrieval قبل أي توليد.[^64_1]

***

## 1) `app/agents/router.py`

المرجع عندك يصف RouterAgent يخرج:
`intent, confidence, language, requiresretrieval, subintent, entities, reasoning, nextaction` ويستخدم LLM + fallback keyword rules + patterns للـ GUID/shortid.[^64_1]

### نموذج الـ Intent

```python
# app/models/intents.py
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field


class UserIntent(BaseModel):
    intent: str = Field(description="One of FIQH, QURAN, ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE, GREETING, ZAKAT, INHERITANCE, DUA, HIJRICALENDAR, PRAYERTIMES")
    confidence: float = Field(description="Confidence score between 0 and 1")
    language: str = Field(description="ar or en")
    requiresretrieval: bool = Field(description="Whether RAG retrieval is needed")
    subintent: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, description="Sub-intent for specific cases like QURAN_VERSELOOKUP")
    entities: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Extracted entities like author, book, category, guid, shortid")
    reasoning: str = Field(description="Brief explanation of classification")
    nextaction: str = Field(description="metadataonly, retrieval, calculator, sqllookup, tool")
```


### RouterAgent

```python
# app/agents/router.py
import re
import json
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from pydantic import ValidationError

from transformers import AutoTokenizer, AutoModelForCausalLM, pipeline
from langchain_core.output_parsers import JsonOutputParser
from langchain_core.prompts import ChatPromptTemplate

from app.core.config import settings
from app.models.intents import UserIntent


GUID_PATTERN = re.compile(
    r"[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}",
    re.IGNORECASE,
)
SHORTID_PATTERN = re.compile(r"[0-9A-F]{6}")
NUMBER_PATTERN = re.compile(r"\d{1,3}(?:[.,]\d{3})*(?:[.,]\d+)?")

INTENT_EXAMPLES = {
    "ZAKAT": ["زكاة", "كم زكاة", "حساب الزكاة", "زكاة المال"],
    "INHERITANCE": ["ميراث", "الورثة", "التركة", "نصيب الزوجة"],
    "QURAN": ["ما معنى قوله تعالى", "سورة البقرة آية", "تفسير آية الكرسي"],
    "DUA": ["دعاء", "ما هو الدعاء", "اذكر دعاء"],
    "PRAYERTIMES": ["مواقيت الصلاة", "وقت صلاة الفجر في"],
    "HIJRICALENDAR": ["التاريخ الهجري", "تحويل من الميلادي إلى الهجري"],
    "GREETING": ["السلام عليكم", "مرحبا", "أهلاً"],
    "FIQH": ["حكم", "ما حكم", "هل يجوز", "الواجب", "الحرام"],
    "ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE": ["من هو", "ما هو الإسلام", "ما هي أركان الإيمان"],
}


class RouterAgent:
    def __init__(self, llm=None):
        self.llm = llm or self._load_llm()
        self.parser = JsonOutputParser(pydantic_object=UserIntent)

    def _load_llm(self):
        tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained("Qwen/Qwen2.5-0.5B-Instruct")
        model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(
            "Qwen/Qwen2.5-0.5B-Instruct",
            device_map="auto",
            torch_dtype="auto",
        )
        pipe = pipeline(
            "text-generation",
            model=model,
            tokenizer=tokenizer,
            max_new_tokens=256,
            temperature=0.1,
            do_sample=False,
            pad_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id,
        )
        return pipe

    def _build_prompt(self, query: str) -> str:
        template = ChatPromptTemplate.from_messages(
            [
                (
                    "system",
                    (
                        "You are an Islamic query classifier and router.\n"
                        "Classify the user query into one of the intents:\n"
                        "FIQH, QURAN, ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE, GREETING, ZAKAT, INHERITANCE, DUA, HIJRICALENDAR, PRAYERTIMES.\n"
                        "Decide:\n"
                        "- language (ar/en)\n"
                        "- requiresretrieval (true/false)\n"
                        "- subintent (e.g., QURAN_VERSELOOKUP)\n"
                        "- entities (author, book, category, guid, shortid, amounts, etc.)\n"
                        "- nextaction: one of metadataonly, retrieval, calculator, sqllookup, tool\n"
                        "Return ONLY a JSON object matching the following schema:\n"
                        "{intent: str, confidence: float, language: str, requiresretrieval: bool, "
                        "subintent: str|null, entities: object, reasoning: str, nextaction: str}"
                    ),
                ),
                ("human", "Query: {query}\nAnswer:"),
            ]
        )
        return template.format_prompt(query=query).to_string()

    def _llm_classify(self, query: str) -> Optional[UserIntent]:
        prompt = self._build_prompt(query)
        raw = self.llm(prompt)[^64_0]["generated_text"]
        # حاول استخراج JSON
        try:
            json_str = raw[raw.index("{") : raw.rindex("}") + 1]
            data = json.loads(json_str)
            return UserIntent(**data)
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _fallback(self, query: str) -> UserIntent:
        ql = query.lower()

        # greeting
        if any(w in ql for w in ["السلام عليكم", "مرحبا", "اهلا", "أهلاً"]):
            return UserIntent(
                intent="GREETING",
                confidence=0.95,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=False,
                subintent=None,
                entities={},
                reasoning="Greeting detected via keywords.",
                nextaction="metadataonly",
            )

        # zakat
        if any(w in ql for w in ["زكاة", "زكات", "حساب الزكاة"]):
            numbers = [n.replace(",", "") for n in NUMBER_PATTERN.findall(query)]
            return UserIntent(
                intent="ZAKAT",
                confidence=0.9,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=False,
                subintent=None,
                entities={"amounts": [float(x) for x in numbers] if numbers else []},
                reasoning="Zakat calculation keywords detected.",
                nextaction="calculator",
            )

        # inheritance
        if any(w in ql for w in ["ميراث", "الورثة", "التركة"]):
            return UserIntent(
                intent="INHERITANCE",
                confidence=0.9,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=False,
                subintent=None,
                entities={},
                reasoning="Inheritance calculation keywords detected.",
                nextaction="calculator",
            )

        # Quran
        if any(w in ql for w in ["قال تعالى", "قوله تعالى", "سورة", "آية", "الاية", "الآية"]):
            return UserIntent(
                intent="QURAN",
                confidence=0.85,
                language="ar",
                requiresretrieval=True,
                subintent="QURAN_INTERPRETATION",
                entities={},
                reasoning="Quran-related keywords detected.",
                nextaction="retrieval",
            )

        # default FIQH / ISLAMIC
        if any(w in ql for w in ["حكم", "يجوز", "لا يجوز", "واجب", "حرام"]):
            base_intent = "FIQH"
        else:
            base_intent = "ISLAMICKNOWLEDGE"

        return UserIntent(
            intent=base_intent,
            confidence=0.7,
            language="ar",
            requiresretrieval=True,
            subintent=None,
            entities={},
            reasoning="Fallback based on general fiqh/knowledge keywords.",
            nextaction="retrieval",
        )

    def _extract_ids(self, query: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        guid_match = GUID_PATTERN.search(query)
        shortid_match = SHORTID_PATTERN.search(query)
        entities: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if guid_match:
            entities["guid"] = guid_match.group(0)
        if shortid_match:
            entities["shortid"] = shortid_match.group(0)
        return entities

    def classify(self, query: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        # 1) حاول LLM
        intent = self._llm_classify(query)
        if not intent or intent.confidence < settings.CONFIDENCETHRESHOLD:
            intent = self._fallback(query)

        # 2) أضف guid/shortid لو موجود
        ids = self._extract_ids(query)
        if ids:
            intent.entities.update(ids)
            if "guid" in ids or "shortid" in ids:
                intent.nextaction = "metadataonly"
                intent.requiresretrieval = False

        return intent.model_dump()
```

هذا يلتزم بما في المرجع من حيث الحقول، مع fallback منطقي يعتمد على الكلمات المفتاحية التي ذكرها.[^64_1]

***

## 2) LangGraph nodes الأساسية

المرجع يصف graph يتكون من:
`route -> author -> category -> book -> plan -> retrieve -> rerank -> answer`.[^64_1]
سنبدأ بنسخة مبسطة (route + plan + retrieve + answer لاحقًا)، مع state هو `GraphState` الذي أنشأناه.

### `app/graph/nodes.py`

```python
# app/graph/nodes.py
from typing import Dict, Any
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.models.agentstate import GraphState
from app.agents.router import RouterAgent
from app.services.retrieval import RetrievalPlanner, RetrievalService


router_agent = RouterAgent()
retrieval_service = RetrievalService()


def route_node(state: GraphState) -> GraphState:
    intent = router_agent.classify(state["query"])
    return {
        "intent": intent,
        "normalizedquery": state["query"].strip(),
    }


def plan_node(state: GraphState, db: Session) -> GraphState:
    planner = RetrievalPlanner(db)
    plan = planner.create_plan(state["intent"])
    candidates = planner.get_candidate_books(plan)
    return {
        "retrievalplan": plan,
        "bookcandidates": [{"bookid": b.bookid} for b in candidates],
    }


def retrieve_node(state: GraphState) -> GraphState:
    plan = state.get("retrievalplan", {})
    query = state["query"]
    chunks = retrieval_service.search(query=query, plan=plan)
    return {"retrievalchunks": chunks}
```

لاحقًا سنضيف:

- `rerank_node` (باستخدام `RERANKERMODEL`).[^64_1]
- `answer_node` (مع AnswerAgent).[^64_1]

***

## 3) `app/graph/builder.py`

المرجع يعطي مثالًا لـ `StateGraph` من LangGraph مع nodes وedges.[^64_1]
نبدأ بـ route → plan → retrieve فقط؛ ثم نضيف rerank/answer لاحقًا.

```python
# app/graph/builder.py
from langgraph.graph import StateGraph, END
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.models.agentstate import GraphState
from app.graph.nodes import route_node, plan_node, retrieve_node


def build_graph(db: Session):
    graph = StateGraph(GraphState)

    # route
    def route_wrapper(state: GraphState) -> GraphState:
        return route_node(state)

    # plan
    def plan_wrapper(state: GraphState) -> GraphState:
        return plan_node(state, db=db)

    # retrieve
    def retrieve_wrapper(state: GraphState) -> GraphState:
        return retrieve_node(state)

    graph.add_node("route", route_wrapper)
    graph.add_node("plan", plan_wrapper)
    graph.add_node("retrieve", retrieve_wrapper)

    graph.set_entry_point("route")
    graph.add_edge("route", "plan")
    graph.add_edge("plan", "retrieve")
    graph.add_edge("retrieve", END)

    return graph.compile()
```

بعدها عندما نضيف AnswerAgent سنضيف `answer` node وedge إضافي.[^64_1]

***

## 4) ربط الـ graph مع FastAPI في `app/api/qa.py`

المرجع يصف endpoint `/qa` أو `/query` يستدعي الـ graph ويقيس latency ويجمع citations.[^64_1]

```python
# app/api/qa.py
import time
from typing import Optional
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.core.db import get_db
from app.models.schemas import QueryRequest, QueryResponse, Citation
from app.models.agentstate import GraphState
from app.graph.builder import build_graph

router = APIRouter(prefix="/qa", tags=["qa"])


@router.post("/plan")
def plan_only(request: QueryRequest, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    app_graph = build_graph(db=db)
    state: GraphState = {"query": request.query}
    start = time.time()
    result = app_graph.invoke(state)
    latency = (time.time() - start) * 1000

    return {
        "intent": result.get("intent"),
        "retrievalplan": result.get("retrievalplan"),
        "bookcandidates": result.get("bookcandidates"),
        "retrievalchunks_count": len(result.get("retrievalchunks", [])),
        "latencyms": latency,
    }
```

حاليًا هذا endpoint فقط يريك planning + retrieval بدون generation.
لاحقًا نضيف endpoint كامل `POST /qa/ask` الذي يعيد جوابًا فعليًا باستخدام AnswerAgent.[^64_1]

***

## 5) تحديث `app/main.py` لضم الـ QA router

```python
# app/main.py (إضافة)
from app.api import qa

app.include_router(qa.router)
```
